    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/moment.js/2.29.4/moment-with-locales.min.js" integrity="sha512-42PE0rd+wZ2hNXftlM78BSehIGzezNeQuzihiBCvUEB3CVxHvsShF86wBWwQORNxNINlBPuq7rG4WWhNiTVHFg==" crossorigin="anonymous"></script>

<script>
moment.locale("en");
function flask_moment_render(elem) {{
    const timestamp = moment(elem.dataset.timestamp);
    const func = elem.dataset.function;
    const format = elem.dataset.format;
    const timestamp2 = elem.dataset.timestamp2;
    const no_suffix = elem.dataset.nosuffix;
    const units = elem.dataset.units;
    let args = [];
    if (format)
        args.push(format);
    if (timestamp2)
        args.push(moment(timestamp2));
    if (no_suffix)
        args.push(no_suffix);
    if (units)
        args.push(units);
    elem.textContent = timestamp[func].apply(timestamp, args);
    elem.classList.remove('flask-moment');
    elem.style.display = "";
}}
function flask_moment_render_all() {{
    const moments = document.querySelectorAll('.flask-moment');
    moments.forEach(function(moment) {{
        flask_moment_render(moment);
        const refresh = moment.dataset.refresh;
        if (refresh && refresh > 0) {{
            (function(elem, interval) {{
                setInterval(function() {{
                    flask_moment_render(elem);
                }}, interval);
            }})(moment, refresh);
        }}
    }})
}}
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", flask_moment_render_all);
</script>

<script>
var global_location_name = "";
var global_view_type = "calendar";
var global_logo_url = "";
function set_logo(url){
  global_logo_url = url;
  document.getElementById("previewLogoImage").src = url;

  if (!url){
    document.getElementById("previewLogoImage").style.display = "none";
    document.getElementById("icon-business-no-logo").style.display = "block";
  }else{
    document.getElementById("previewLogoImage").style.display = "block";
    document.getElementById("icon-business-no-logo").style.display = "none";
  }

}


function get_logo_url(callback){
  $.ajax({
            data: {
                get_logo: true,
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href,
        })
        .done(function(data) {
         
          set_logo(data.url);
          if (callback){
            callback();
          }

        });
}


function requestEvolution(businessId) {
  global_logo_url = "";
    reset_modal_and_new_post_data();
    //$("#switchEvolutionId").bootstrapSwitch('disabled',true);
    document.getElementById("dropdownMenuButtonActionsID").classList.add("disabled");
    //Put the name of the location to the div
    businessName = $("#" + businessId + " .location-name").text();
    document.getElementById("business-id-handler").innerHTML = businessId;

    var mode_tmp = "1";
    //if ($('#switchEvolutionId').bootstrapSwitch('state')){
      //  mode_tmp = "2";
    //}

    if (businessName == "") {
        businessName = translations["Selecionar Local GBP"];
    }
    document.getElementById("selected-gmb-profile").innerHTML = businessName + "<i class='fa-solid fa-caret-down drop-right'></i>";

    global_location_name = businessName;

    $.ajax({
            data: {
                change_business: businessId,
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href,
        })
        .done(function(data) {
          change_posts_view_type(global_view_type);
            // get_posts_for_dates_interval();
            generate_post_ideas();
            get_latlng();

            document.getElementById("dropdownMenuButtonActionsID").classList.remove("disabled");


          get_logo_url(

            function(){
              document.querySelectorAll(".preview-img-post-list").forEach(function(item){
                item.src = global_logo_url;
              });

            }

          ); 
        


        });
}
</script>

            <script>
                var can_use_arrows = false;

                // Version filter: saved preference
                var savedVersionFilter = 'all';

                // Show version filter switch only if both V1 and V2 items exist
                $(document).ready(function() {
                    var hasV1 = document.querySelectorAll('#list .v1-item').length > 0;
                    var hasV2 = document.querySelectorAll('#list .selectable:not(.v1-item), #list .location-item:not(.v1-item)').length > 0;
                    if (hasV1 && hasV2) {
                        document.getElementById('version-filter-switch').style.display = 'block';
                        document.getElementById('version-filter-switch').dataset.hasVersions = 'true';

                        // Load saved preference
                        $.get('/extension-v2/preference', { pref_key: 'version_filter' }, function(data) {
                            if (data.value && ['all', 'v1', 'v2'].indexOf(data.value) !== -1) {
                                savedVersionFilter = data.value;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    // Prevent dropdown close when clicking the switch
                    var versionFilterSwitch = document.getElementById('version-filter-switch');
                    if (versionFilterSwitch) {
                        versionFilterSwitch.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                        });
                    }
                    document.querySelectorAll('.version-switch-input').forEach(function(input) {
                        input.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            // Save preference
                            $.post('/extension-v2/preference', {
                                pref_key: 'version_filter',
                                pref_value: e.target.value
                            });
                            savedVersionFilter = e.target.value;
                            filterFunction();
                        });
                    });
                });

                $('#mainDropdownID').on('show.bs.dropdown', function() {
                    document.getElementById("myInput").value = "";
                    // Restore saved preference
                    var switchId = 'switch-' + savedVersionFilter;
                    var el = document.getElementById(switchId);
                    if (el) el.checked = true;
                    lastVersionFilter = savedVersionFilter;
                    filterFunction();
                })
                $('#mainDropdownID').on('shown.bs.dropdown', function() {
                    $("#mainDropdownID").data("open", true);
                    document.getElementById("myInput").focus();
                    document.getElementById("myInput").value = "";

                    if (document.getElementById("locations-dropdown-input")){
                        document.getElementById("locations-dropdown-input").focus();
                    }
                    can_use_arrows = true;
                })
                $("#mainDropdownID").on("hidden.bs.dropdown", function() {
                    $(this).data("open", false);
                    can_use_arrows = false;

                    if (liSelected) {
                        liSelected.classList.remove('background');
                    }
                    liSelected = undefined;
                    selected = undefined;
                    next = -1;
                    liList = undefined;
                    lastData = "";
                });



            </script>

<script>
    var is_weekly = false;
    var date_range = null;
    var editing_post = null;
var state;

       


    state = new Proxy({ post_now: true }, {
      set(target, property, value) {
          if (property === 'post_now') {
              let schedule_text = editing_post ? translations["Salvar Agendamento"]  : translations["Agendar Publicação"];
              document.getElementById("publish_now").innerText = value ? translations["Publicar Agora"] : schedule_text;

          }
          target[property] = value;
          return true;
      }
  });





    let place_id = document.getElementById("business-id-handler").innerHTML;
  if (place_id)
  {
      change_name_of_current_business(place_id);
  }
</script>

<script>
function get_business_name(){
    let place_id = document.getElementById("business-id-handler").innerText;
    if (place_id)
    {
      const selector = `[id="${place_id}"] .location-name`;
      return document.querySelector(selector).innerText;
    }

    return "";
}
function renderEventsListView(events) {
    const listView = document.querySelector("#listView");
    if (!listView) return;

    if (!events.length) {
        listView.innerHTML = `
        
        <div style="width:100%; margin-top:100px;"><h3 style="font-weight:bold; text-align:center;font-size:24px;">Gerenciador de atualizações</h3><br><div style="width:100%; display: flex; justify-content: center;"><i style="font-size:48px;" class="icon-megaphone"></i></div><br><br><h5 style="text-align:center; font-size:17px; margin-bottom:100px;">Ainda não existem atualizações criadas</h5></div>
        
        `;
        return;
    }

    // Função auxiliar para formatar a data, hora e tempo decorrido
    function formatDate(dateString) {
        const options = { weekday: 'long', month: 'long', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' };
        const date = new Date(dateString);
        return date.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', options);
    }

    function formatTime(dateString) {
        const date = new Date(dateString);
        const hours = String(date.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
        const minutes = String(date.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
        return `${hours}:${minutes}`;
    }

    function calculateTimeElapsed(dateString) {
    const eventDate = new Date(dateString);
    const now = new Date();
    const diffInMinutes = Math.floor((now - eventDate) / 60000); // Diferença em minutos

    if (diffInMinutes < 60) {
        return `há ${diffInMinutes} minuto${diffInMinutes === 1 ? "" : "s"}`;
    }

    const diffInHours = Math.floor(diffInMinutes / 60);
    if (diffInHours < 24) {
        return `há ${diffInHours} hora${diffInHours === 1 ? "" : "s"}`;
    }

    const diffInDays = Math.floor(diffInHours / 24);
    return `há ${diffInDays} dia${diffInDays === 1 ? "" : "s"}`;
}


    // Agrupa os eventos por dia usando schedule_date
    const groupedEvents = events.reduce((acc, event) => {
        const key_for_date = event.schedule_date ? event.schedule_date : event.moment_of_submission;
        const dateKey = formatDate(key_for_date);
        if (!acc[dateKey]) acc[dateKey] = [];
        acc[dateKey].push(event);
        return acc;
    }, {});

    // Ordena os dias e os eventos dentro de cada dia
    const sortedDates = Object.keys(groupedEvents).sort((a, b) => new Date(a) - new Date(b));
    sortedDates.forEach(dateKey => {
        groupedEvents[dateKey].sort((a, b) => new Date(a.schedule_date) - new Date(b.schedule_date));
    });

    // Cria o HTML para cada dia e seus eventos
    const eventsHTML = sortedDates.map(dateKey => {
        const eventsForDay = groupedEvents[dateKey];
        const dateLabel = `<div style="font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px;">${dateKey}</div>`;

        const location_name = get_business_name();

        const eventsForDayHTML = eventsForDay.map(event => {
          if (!event.schedule_date){
                event.schedule_date = event.moment_of_submission;
              }
              
              console.log("dddd",event.schedule_date);

            const time = formatTime(event.schedule_date)

            console.log("time",time);
            const elapsed = calculateTimeElapsed(event.moment_of_submission);
            const created_text = event.moment_of_submission ? translations["Você criou este post"] + " " + elapsed : "";
            const description = event.summary || "";

            let additional_options = `
    <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px;">
        <button class="list-view-publish-now" data-list-post-id='${event.id}' 
            style="border: none; background-color: #00aa66; color: #fff; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 4px; cursor: pointer;">
            ${translations["Publicar Agora"]}
        </button>
        <button data-list-post-id="${event.id}" class="list-edit-post" 
            style="border: 1px solid #00aa66;color: #00aa66;background-color: white;padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 4px;">
            ${translations["Editar"]}
        </button>
        <div class="dropdown">
            <button id="more_options_btn" style="border: 1px solid #00aa66; color: #00aa66; background-color: white; padding: 5px 10px; border-radius: 4px;" 
                class="btn " type="button" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-expanded="false">
                <i class="icon-more2"></i>
            </button>
            <div class="dropdown-menu small-drop-menu">
                <a style="color:#d33d44;" data-delete-post-list="${event.id}" class="dropdown-item" href="#">
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i> ${translations["Apagar"]}
                </a>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
`;


            if (event.status == "SUCCESS" || event.status == "SENDING") {




              additional_options = `
    <div style="display: flex; gap: 16px; align-items:center;">
        <span> 
            ${translations["Publicado em"]} ${formatDate(event.schedule_date)} ${translations["às"]} ${formatTime(event.schedule_date)}
        </span>

        <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; align-items:end;">
            <a class='btn' style='color:#0099ee;  border:1px solid #0099ee; background-color:white; padding: 2px 8px; cursor:pointer;' 
                onclick=get_post_for_edition('${event.id}'); target='_blank'>
                ${translations["Ver Preview"]}
            </a>
            <a class='btn' style='background-color:#0099ee; color:white; padding: 2px 8px;' 
                href='${event.postSearchUrl}' target='_blank'>
                ${translations["Ver no Google"]}
            </a>
        </div>
    </div>
`;

            }else if (event.status == "ERROR") {
              additional_options = `
              <div style="display: flex; gap: 16px; align-items:center;">
                                    <b style="color:#d33d44;"> 
                                      ${translations["Erro ao publicar"]}
                                      </b>

              </div>
              
              `;
            }else if (event.status == "RETRY") {
              additional_options = `
              <div style="display: flex; gap: 16px; align-items:center;">
                                    <b style="color:#FF6600;"> 
                                      ${translations["Tentando novamente..."] || "Tentando novamente..."}
                                      </b>

              </div>
              
              `;
            }

            return `
                <div style="margin-bottom: 20px; display: flex; align-items: flex-start;">
                    <!-- Linha do tempo na esquerda -->
                    <div style="width: 45px; text-align: right; margin-right: 20px; font-size: 14px;">
                        <div>${time}</div>
                    </div>
                    <!-- Cartão do evento -->
                    <div style="flex: 1;">
                        <div style="border: 1px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; padding: 10px;">
                            <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 10px;">
                                <img class="preview-img-post-list" style="width:40px; height: 40px; border-radius: 50%;" src="${global_logo_url}" alt="">
                                <div style="font-weight: bold; margin-left:10px;">${location_name}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div style="padding: 20px;">${description}</div>
                            <hr style="border: none; border-top: 1px solid #ddd; margin: 10px 0;">
                            <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: space-between;">
                                <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #555;">${created_text}</div>
                                ${additional_options}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
        }).join("");

        return `${dateLabel}${eventsForDayHTML}`;
    }).join("");

    // Adiciona o HTML no elemento listView
    listView.innerHTML = eventsHTML;

    // Adiciona o listener para os botões de editar
    document.querySelectorAll(".list-edit-post").forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener("click", event => {
          const postId = event.target.getAttribute("data-list-post-id");
          editing_post = postId;
          get_post_for_edition(postId);
        });
    });


    document.querySelectorAll(".list-view-publish-now").forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener("click", event => {
          const postId = event.target.getAttribute("data-list-post-id");
          publish_existing_post_now(postId);
        });
    });

    // Adiciona o listener para os botões de deletar
    document.querySelectorAll("[data-delete-post-list]").forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener("click", event => {
          const postId = event.target.getAttribute("data-delete-post-list");
          delete_post_by_id(postId);



        });
    });


}


  function change_posts_view_type(type){
    if (type === 'calendar'){
      document.getElementById("calendarViewHolder").style.display = "block";
      document.getElementById("listViewHolder").style.display = "none";

      // enable viewDay, viewWeek, viewMonth
      document.getElementById("viewDay").disabled = false;
      document.getElementById("viewWeek").disabled = false;
      document.getElementById("viewMonth").disabled = false;

      // enable prev, next, today
      document.getElementById("prev").disabled = false;
      document.getElementById("next").disabled = false;
      document.getElementById("today").disabled = false;

      document.getElementById("posts-view-type-change-btn").textContent = translations["Calendário"];

      get_posts_for_dates_interval();

      global_view_type = "calendar";

    } else {
      document.getElementById("calendarViewHolder").style.display = "none";
      document.getElementById("listViewHolder").style.display = "block";

      // disable viewDay, viewWeek, viewMonth
      document.getElementById("viewDay").disabled = true;
      document.getElementById("viewWeek").disabled = true;
      document.getElementById("viewMonth").disabled = true;

      // disable prev, next, today
      document.getElementById("prev").disabled = true;
      document.getElementById("next").disabled = true;
      document.getElementById("today").disabled = true;

      document.getElementById("posts-view-type-change-btn").textContent = translations["Lista"];

      get_posts_for_list_view();

      global_view_type = "list";
      
    }
  }

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-posts-visualization]").forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener("click", event => {
      change_posts_view_type(event.target.getAttribute("data-posts-visualization"));
    });
  });
  
</script>

<script>



var calendar;


function removeAllEvents(){
    const events = document.querySelectorAll(".post-event");
    events.forEach(event => {
        event.remove();
    });
}



function AddEventListToCalendar(eventList) {
    // Verifica se a lista é válida
    if (!Array.isArray(eventList) || eventList.length === 0) {
      set_calendar_dimensions();
        console.warn("A lista de eventos está vazia ou não é válida.");
        return;
    }

    // Itera sobre a lista de eventos e chama addEventToCalendar para cada um
    eventList.forEach(event => {
        if (event.start) {
            addEventToCalendar(event);
        } else {
            console.warn(`Evento inválido ignorado:`, event);
        }
    });


    const eventElements = document.querySelectorAll(".post-event");
    eventElements.forEach(eventElement => {
      eventElement.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      //prevent event from bubbling up
      event.stopPropagation();
      event.preventDefault();


        editing_post = eventElement.id;
        get_post_for_edition(eventElement.id);
    });


      // Torna o elemento arrastável
      // se o event estiver numa célula date-past, retornar
      console.log("eventElement", eventElement.parentElement);
      if (eventElement.parentElement.classList.contains("date-past") && (currentView != "day")) {
          return;
      }

      if (eventElement.parentElement.parentElement.classList.contains("date-past") && (currentView == "day")) {
          return;
      }


      eventElement.setAttribute("draggable", "true");

// Define o comportamento ao iniciar o arrasto
eventElement.addEventListener("dragstart", (e) => {
    e.dataTransfer.setData("text/plain", eventElement.id); // Envia o ID do elemento
    eventElement.classList.add("dragging"); // Adiciona uma classe opcional para estilo
});

// Remove a classe de estilo ao terminar o arrasto
eventElement.addEventListener("dragend", () => {
    eventElement.classList.remove("dragging");
});


    });




    const cells = document.querySelectorAll("tbody td");


// Permite que as células recebam elementos arrastados
cells.forEach(cell => {
    cell.addEventListener("dragover", (e) => {
        e.preventDefault(); // Necessário para permitir o drop
        cell.classList.add("drag-over"); // Classe opcional para estilo ao arrastar
    });

    cell.addEventListener("dragleave", () => {
        cell.classList.remove("drag-over"); // Remove a classe ao sair
    });

    // Define o comportamento ao soltar o elemento
    cell.addEventListener("drop", (e) => {
      
        e.preventDefault(); // Previne o comportamento padrão

        

        //se a cell estiver numa date-past, retornar
        if (cell.classList.contains("date-past")) {
            return; 
        }


        const eventId = e.dataTransfer.getData("text/plain");
        const draggedElement = document.getElementById(eventId);

        // Adiciona o elemento arrastado à nova célula
        if (draggedElement && cell !== draggedElement.parentElement) {

          let date = cell.getAttribute("data-date");
          let hour = cell.getAttribute("data-hour");

          console.log("date", date, "hour", hour);

          let new_date_string = `${date}`;

          if (hour){
            // this is a monthly view
            new_date_string = `${date}T${hour}:00`;
          }

          // Combine a data e a hora manualmente
          

          // Atualiza o evento com a nova data
          update_event_date(eventId, new_date_string);

          // Adiciona o evento na célula
          cell.appendChild(draggedElement);

          // Remove a classe de estilo
          cell.classList.remove("drag-over");

      }


        cell.classList.remove("drag-over"); // Remove a classe de estilo
    });
});





    set_calendar_dimensions();
}

function show_only_n_chars(string, n_chars){
    if (string.length > n_chars){
        return string.substring(0, n_chars) + "...";
    }

    return string;
}

function addEventToCalendar(event) {
    const { title, start } = event;

    // Verifica se os parâmetros estão presentes
    if (!start) {
        console.warn("O evento deve conter um título e uma data/hora inicial.");
        return;
    }

// Converte a data/hora para um objeto Date
let eventDateTime = new Date(start);

// Ajusta o horário para UTC considerando o fuso horário local
eventDateTime = new Date(eventDateTime.getTime() + eventDateTime.getTimezoneOffset() * 60000);

// Arredonda os minutos para 0 ou 30
let minutes = eventDateTime.getMinutes();
eventDateTime.setMinutes(minutes < 30 ? 0 : 30);
eventDateTime.setSeconds(0); // Remove segundos para garantir precisão

console.log("eventDateTime", eventDateTime, minutes);

const now = new Date();

// Localiza a célula correspondente no calendário
const cellSelector = `[data-date="${toLocalISOString(eventDateTime).split("T")[0]}"]`;
const cells = document.querySelectorAll(cellSelector);

let targetCell = null;
cells.forEach(cell => {
    const cellHour = cell.getAttribute("data-hour");

    // Verifica se é visualização mensal (sem data-hour)
    if (!cellHour) {
        targetCell = cell; // Para visualização mensal, só importa o data-date
    } else {
        // Para modos diário ou semanal, verifica também a hora
        const eventTime = eventDateTime.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        if (cellHour.trim() === eventTime) {
            targetCell = cell;
        }
    }
});

if (!targetCell) {
    console.warn(`Não foi encontrada uma célula correspondente para o evento: ${title} - ${start}`);
    return;
}

// A célula correspondente foi encontrada
console.log("Célula encontrada:", targetCell);


    // event: {
//     "id": "28a1b7bd-d0f0-4db7-b2d5-a21d1befa3ac",
//     "title": "Atualização (Agendado)",
//     "thumbnail": null,
//     "status": "SCHEDULED",
//     "color": "#0099ee",
//     "textColor": "#ffffff",
//     "start": "2024-11-19T00:00:00.000Z",
//     "end": "2024-11-19T00:00:00.000Z"
// }


// ${
//             event.thumbnail 
//                 ? `<img src="${event.thumbnail}" style="width: auto; height: 34px; margin-top: 4px;">` 
//                 : ''
//         }
//<img style="width:15px;" class="question-img" src="https://www.gstatic.com/images/icons/material/system/2x/store_googblue_48dp.png">

    // Cria o elemento visual do evento
    const html = `
    <div class="post-event post-content-holder" id="${event.id}" style="border: 1px solid ${event.color};">
      <div style="padding-top:0px;">
        
        <i class="fa-solid fa-shop" style="color:${event.color}; font-size: 12px; margin-right: 4px;"></i>

        </div>
        <span class="post-title">
          ${title ? show_only_n_chars(title, 15) : "<i>"+translations["(Sem Texto)"]+"</i>"}
        </span>
 
    </div>
`;

// Adiciona o evento na célula
targetCell.innerHTML += html;


    console.log(`Evento adicionado em: ${start}`);
}


function addEventToCalendarCell(cell, title) {
    // Cria o elemento visual do evento
    const eventElement = document.createElement("div");
    eventElement.textContent = title;
    eventElement.style.backgroundColor = "#007bff";
    eventElement.style.color = "white";
    eventElement.style.borderRadius = "4px";
    eventElement.style.padding = "2px 4px";
    eventElement.style.margin = "2px 0";
    eventElement.style.fontSize = "10px";
    eventElement.style.textAlign = "center";
    eventElement.style.overflow = "hidden";
    eventElement.style.textOverflow = "ellipsis"; // Adiciona "..." caso o texto exceda o espaço disponível
    eventElement.style.whiteSpace = "nowrap";

    // Impede mudanças de largura da célula
    cell.style.padding = "8px";
    cell.style.height = "auto";
    cell.appendChild(eventElement);
}



function addNewPostButtonToCell(cell) {

  //if cell alreay has a button, do not add another
  if (cell.querySelector(".add-new-event")) {
      return;
  }




    // Cria o elemento visual do evento
    const eventElement = document.createElement("div");
    eventElement.classList.add("add-new-event");
    eventElement.style.backgroundColor = "transparent";
    eventElement.style.color = "#0099ee";
    eventElement.style.borderRadius = "4px";
    eventElement.style.border = "1px solid #0099ee";
    eventElement.style.height = "48px";
    eventElement.style.margin = "4px 0px";
    // text content vertical center
    eventElement.style.display = "flex";
    eventElement.style.alignItems = "center";
    eventElement.style.justifyContent = "center";
    eventElement.style.cursor = "pointer";

    const text = document.createElement("span");
    text.textContent = "+";
    text.style.fontSize = "18px";
    text.style.borderRadius = "4px";
    text.style.padding = "1px 8px";
    // text.style.border = "1px solid #0099ee";

    eventElement.appendChild(text);







    // Impede mudanças de largura da célula
    cell.style.padding = "8px";
    cell.style.height = "auto";
    cell.appendChild(eventElement);

    // tooltip  
    eventElement.setAttribute("data-toggle", "tooltip");
    eventElement.setAttribute("data-placement", "top");
    eventElement.setAttribute("title", translations["Adicionar Postagem"]);


   // Inicializa o tooltip com delay configurado
$(eventElement).tooltip({
    delay: { show: 300, hide: 0 } // Delay de 500ms para exibir, 100ms para ocultar
});

eventElement.addEventListener("click", () => {

  if (editing_post){

    reset_modal_and_new_post_data();
  }

  open_new_post_modal_for_new_schedule(cell);

});

   

}



function open_new_post_modal_for_new_schedule(cell){
  document.getElementById('card-success').style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById('card-scheduled').style.display = "flex";

  const cellDate = cell.getAttribute("data-date");
            let cellHour = cell.getAttribute("data-hour");
            
            if (!cellHour){
                cellHour = "08:00"; // Define uma hora padrão para o evento
            }
            console.log(`Célula clicada: ${cellDate} ${cellHour ? cellHour.trim() : ""}`);

            if (cellDate) {
                // Se há hora associada, combine data e hora
                const clickedDateTime = cellHour
                    ? new Date(`${cellDate}T${cellHour.trim()}:00`) // Formato completo de data e hora
                    : new Date(cellDate); // Apenas a data

                    const now = new Date();

                // if hours is the same but minutes are higher now, set to now 
                if (clickedDateTime.getHours() === now.getHours() && now.getMinutes() > clickedDateTime.getMinutes()) {
                    clickedDateTime.setMinutes(now.getMinutes()+5);
                }
                



                
                //now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); // Remove horas para comparar apenas datas

                // Validação para datas passadas
                if (clickedDateTime < now) {
                  // if view == month and date.day == today.day, set the time to now + 5 minutes
                  if (currentView == "month" && clickedDateTime.getDate() === now.getDate()){
                    clickedDateTime.setMinutes(now.getMinutes() + 5);
                  } else {

                    console.warn(`Já passou: ${cellHour ? `${cellDate} ${cellHour.trim()}` : cellDate}`);
                    return; // Não faz mais nada
                  }
                }

                    let selectedDate = moment(clickedDateTime);
                    state.post_now = false;
                    $('input[name="birthday"]').val(selectedDate.format('DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm'));
                    $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setStartDate(selectedDate);
                    $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setEndDate(selectedDate);

                    editing_post = null;
                    $('#postModal').modal('show');



                // Adiciona o evento na célula correspondente
                // addEventToCalendarCell(cell, "Atualização");
                console.log(`Evento sendo criado em: ${cellHour ? `${cellDate} ${cellHour.trim()}` : cellDate}`);
            }
}


function attachCellEventHandlers() {
    const cells = document.querySelectorAll(".day-view td, .week-view td, .month-view td");

    cells.forEach(cell => {
        cell.addEventListener("click", () => {
            
        });



        // event on hover
        // add an event button to the cell
        // class must be add-new-event, musb be a transparent div with a plus icon centered in the cell, when clicked, it will open the modal to create a new event
        cell.addEventListener("mouseover", () => {

          // if cell has date-past, do not add button
          if (cell.classList.contains("date-past")) {
              return;
          }

          if (currentView == "day"){
            if (cell.parentElement.classList.contains("date-past")) {
                return;
            }
          }



            const cellDate = cell.getAttribute("data-date");
            let cellHour = cell.getAttribute("data-hour");
            if (!cellHour){
                cellHour = "08:00"; // Define uma hora padrão para o evento
            }


            if (cellDate) {
                // Se há hora associada, combine data e hora
                const clickedDateTime = cellHour
                    ? new Date(`${cellDate}T${cellHour.trim()}:00`) // Formato completo de data e hora
                    : new Date(cellDate); // Apenas a data

                const now = new Date();
                now.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); // Remove horas para comparar apenas datas

                // Validação para datas passadas
                if (clickedDateTime < now) {
                    //console.warn(`Já passou: ${cellHour ? `${cellDate} ${cellHour.trim()}` : cellDate}`);
                    return; // Não faz mais nada
                }

                // Adiciona o evento na célula correspondente
                addNewPostButtonToCell(cell);
            }
            
        });

        // on mouse leave, remove button for the cell
        cell.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => {

            const addNewEvent = cell.querySelector(".add-new-event");
            // remove tooltip
            $(addNewEvent).tooltip('dispose');

            if (addNewEvent) {
                addNewEvent.remove();
            }
        });






    });
}



function toLocalDate(dateString) {
    return new Date(dateString); // Construtor do JavaScript interpreta automaticamente o fuso horário.
}


function renderNowIndicatorForDay() {
    const now = new Date();
    const currentHour = now.getHours();
    const currentMinutes = now.getMinutes();

    // Verificar se o dia exibido corresponde ao dia atual
    const displayedDate = document.querySelector(".day-view").dataset.date; // Obtemos o dia exibido
    if (displayedDate !== toLocalISOString(now).split("T")[0]) {
        document.querySelectorAll(".now-indicator, .now-indicator-arrow").forEach(el => el.remove());
        return; // Não renderizar indicador se não for o dia atual
    }

    const tableRows = document.querySelectorAll(".day-view tbody tr");
    const totalMinutes = currentHour * 60 + currentMinutes; // Total de minutos desde a meia-noite
    const rowIndex = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 30); // Índice da linha para intervalos de 30 minutos

    const currentRow = tableRows[rowIndex]; // Linha correspondente ao intervalo atual

    if (currentRow) {
        // Remove qualquer indicador anterior
        document.querySelectorAll(".now-indicator, .now-indicator-arrow").forEach(el => el.remove());

        // Obter altura da célula para ajustar a posição do indicador
        const rowHeight = currentRow.offsetHeight;
        const positionWithinRow = (currentMinutes % 30) / 30 * rowHeight; // Posição dentro da linha baseada nos minutos

        // Cria a seta no canto esquerdo
        const arrowIndicator = document.createElement("div");
        arrowIndicator.className = "now-indicator-arrow";
        arrowIndicator.style.position = "absolute";
        arrowIndicator.style.top = `${positionWithinRow}px`; // Posição ajustada
        arrowIndicator.style.left = "-10px";
        arrowIndicator.style.width = "20px";
        arrowIndicator.style.height = "20px";
        arrowIndicator.style.backgroundColor = "red";
        arrowIndicator.style.clipPath = "polygon(0 0, 100% 50%, 0 100%)";

        const firstCell = currentRow.querySelector("td");
        if (firstCell) {
            firstCell.style.position = "relative"; // Certifique-se de que a célula permite posicionamento absoluto
            firstCell.appendChild(arrowIndicator);
        }

        // Cria o indicador de linha
        const indicator = document.createElement("div");
        indicator.className = "now-indicator";
        indicator.style.position = "absolute";
        indicator.style.top = `${positionWithinRow}px`; // Posição ajustada
        indicator.style.left = "0";
        indicator.style.padding = "0";
        indicator.style.width = "99.6%";
        indicator.style.height = "2px";
        indicator.style.backgroundColor = "red";

        currentRow.style.position = "relative"; // Necessário para posicionamento absoluto
        currentRow.appendChild(indicator);
    }
}


function renderNowIndicatorForWeek() {
    const now = new Date();
    const currentHour = now.getHours();
    const currentMinutes = now.getMinutes();
    const today = toLocalISOString(now).split("T")[0]; // Data atual no formato YYYY-MM-DD

    // Remove qualquer indicador anterior
    document.querySelectorAll(".now-indicator, .now-indicator-arrow").forEach(el => el.remove());

    // Seleciona todas as linhas de 30 minutos
    const tableRows = document.querySelectorAll(".week-view tbody tr");
    const totalMinutes = currentHour * 60 + currentMinutes; // Total de minutos desde a meia-noite
    const rowIndex = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 30); // Índice da linha para intervalos de 30 minutos

    const currentRow = tableRows[rowIndex]; // Linha correspondente ao intervalo atual

    if (currentRow) {
        // Adicionar indicador apenas no dia atual
        const currentDayCell = currentRow.querySelector(`td[data-date="${today}"]`);
        if (currentDayCell) {
            // Obter altura da célula para ajustar a posição do indicador
            const cellHeight = currentDayCell.offsetHeight;
            const positionWithinCell = (currentMinutes % 30) / 30 * cellHeight; // Posição proporcional dentro da célula

            // Cria a linha vermelha no dia atual
            const redLine = document.createElement("div");
            redLine.className = "now-indicator";
            redLine.style.position = "absolute";
            redLine.style.top = `${positionWithinCell}px`; // Posição calculada corretamente
            redLine.style.left = "0";
            redLine.style.height = "2px";
            redLine.style.padding = "0"; // Mantido como 0
            redLine.style.width = "100%";
            redLine.style.backgroundColor = "red";

            currentDayCell.style.position = "relative";
            currentDayCell.appendChild(redLine);

            // Cria a seta no canto esquerdo
            const arrowIndicator = document.createElement("div");
            arrowIndicator.className = "now-indicator-arrow";
            arrowIndicator.style.position = "absolute";
            arrowIndicator.style.top = `${positionWithinCell}px`; // Mesma posição da linha
            arrowIndicator.style.left = "-10px";
            arrowIndicator.style.width = "20px";
            arrowIndicator.style.height = "20px";
            arrowIndicator.style.backgroundColor = "red";
            arrowIndicator.style.clipPath = "polygon(0 0, 100% 50%, 0 100%)";

            const firstCell = currentRow.querySelector("td");
            if (firstCell) {
                firstCell.style.position = "relative";
                firstCell.appendChild(arrowIndicator);
            }
        }
    }
}




let currentDate = new Date();
var currentView = 'month'; // Default view
var start_date_showing = null;
var end_date_showing = null;
// Atualiza o rótulo de intervalo de datas
function updateViewLabel() {
    const label = document.getElementById("currentViewLabel");
    if (currentView === 'day') {
        label.textContent = currentDate.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', {
            day: 'numeric', month: 'long', year: 'numeric'
        });
    } else if (currentView === 'week') {
        const startOfWeek = new Date(currentDate);
        startOfWeek.setDate(currentDate.getDate() - currentDate.getDay());
        const endOfWeek = new Date(startOfWeek);
        endOfWeek.setDate(startOfWeek.getDate() + 6);
        label.textContent = `${startOfWeek.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short' })} – ${endOfWeek.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' })}`;
    } else if (currentView === 'month') {
        label.textContent = currentDate.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', { month: 'long', year: 'numeric' });
    }
}
function get_posts_for_list_view(){
  console.log("requisitando posts para intervalo de datas", date_range);

$.ajax({
    data: {
      get_posts_for_list_view: true,
      post_status: "SCHEDULED",
    },
    type: "POST",
    url: window.location.href
}).done(function(data) {
    console.log("posts for dates",data);

    renderEventsListView(data.posts);

});
}



function get_posts_for_dates_interval(){
        //remove all calendar events
        removeAllEvents();

        date_range = get_start_and_end_date();

        console.log("requisitando posts para intervalo de datas", date_range);

        $.ajax({
            data: {
              get_posts_for_dates_interval: true,
              start_date: date_range.start_date,
              end_date: date_range.end_date
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            console.log("posts for dates",data);

            if (data.success) {
              let events = []
              
              data.posts.forEach(function(post) {
    let post_event = {
        id: post.id,
        //title: status_map[post.topicType] + "<br>(" + status_map[post.status] + ")",
        title: post.summary,

        thumbnail: post.thumbnail,
        status: post.status

    };

    let true_date = post.schedule_date ? post.schedule_date : post.moment_of_submission;
    console.log("true_date", true_date);
    console.log(post.status);

    if (post.status === "SCHEDULED") {
        post_event.color = "#0099ee"; // Define cor do fundo e da borda
        post_event.textColor = "#ffffff"; // Cor do texto para contraste
        post_event.start = toLocalISOString(new Date(post.schedule_date));
        post_event.end = toLocalISOString(new Date(post.schedule_date));
    } else if (post.status === "SUCCESS") {
        post_event.color = "#00aa66"; // Define cor do fundo e da borda
        post_event.textColor = "#ffffff"; // Cor do texto para contraste
        post_event.start = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
        post_event.end = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
    } else if (post.status === "ERROR") {
        post_event.color = "#d9534f"; // Define cor do fundo e da borda
        post_event.textColor = "#ffffff"; // Cor do texto para contraste
        post_event.start = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
        post_event.end = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
    } else if (post.status === "RETRY") {
        post_event.color = "#FF6600"; // Laranja para retry
        post_event.textColor = "#FFFFFF"; // Texto branco para contraste
        post_event.start = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
        post_event.end = toLocalISOString(new Date(true_date));
    }else{
      console.log("NONE status")
    }

    events.push(post_event);
});
      console.log("events to calendar", events);
      AddEventListToCalendar(events);

    }


        });
      }


function set_calendar_dimensions(){




    // set height for rows of minimum of 60px, if there is any event in the row, set the height to ((events*60) + 60)px
    const rows = document.querySelectorAll("tbody tr");

    rows.forEach(row => {

      //if in row there are only cells with date-past class, do not set height
      const rows_td = row.querySelectorAll("td");
      let all_cells_past = true;
      rows_td.forEach(td => {
        //if there is no data-date, ignore
        if (!td.getAttribute("data-date")){
          return;
        }

        if (!td.classList.contains("date-past")){
          all_cells_past = false;
        }
      });

      console.log(all_cells_past)

      if (all_cells_past){
        return;
      }


        //get max number of events in a roll cell
        const row_cells = row.querySelectorAll("td");
        const cells_events = [];
        row_cells.forEach(cell => {
            const events = cell.querySelectorAll(".post-event");
            cells_events.push(events.length);
        });
        const max_events = Math.max(...cells_events);


        const events = max_events;

        if (max_events > 0) {
            console.warn("events", events);
        } else {

        }

        if (events > 0) {
            row.style.height = `${(events * 58) + 58 + 24}px`;
        } else {
          if (currentView==="month"){
            row.style.height = "100px";
          }else{
            row.style.height = "76px";
          }
        }
    });

    if (currentView == 'day'){
      return;
    }


    if (currentView == 'month'){
      //set width of cells to 14.27%
      const cells = document.querySelectorAll("tbody td");
      cells.forEach(cell => {
          cell.style.width = "14.27%";
      });
      return;
    }


    if (currentView === 'week') {
    // Define a largura fixa para a primeira coluna (horário)
    const firstColumn = document.querySelectorAll("tbody td:first-child, thead th:first-child");
    firstColumn.forEach(column => {
        column.style.width = "60px";
    });

    // Ajusta a largura das demais colunas
    const table = document.querySelector("table");
    const totalColumns = table.querySelectorAll("thead th").length - 1; // Exclui a primeira coluna
    const remainingWidth = table.offsetWidth - 60; // Subtrai a largura da primeira coluna
    const cellWidth = `${remainingWidth / totalColumns}px`;

    const otherColumns = document.querySelectorAll("tbody td:not(:first-child), thead th:not(:first-child)");
    otherColumns.forEach(cell => {
        cell.style.width = cellWidth;
    });
}


}






function scrollToNow(){

  const now = new Date();
  const currentHour = now.getHours();
  const currentMinutes = now.getMinutes();

  // get cell with current date on data-date
  const today_cell = document.querySelectorAll(`td[data-date="${toLocalISOString(now).split("T")[0]}"]`);

  if (!today_cell.length){
    return;
  }

  //if view is monthly just scroll to today cell and return
  if (currentView === 'month'){
    //console.log("scrolling to today cell", today_cell);
    //today_cell[0].scrollIntoView();
    return;
  }



  setTimeout(() => {
// Scroll to .now-indicator relative to #calendarViewHolder
const now_indicator = document.querySelector(".now-indicator");
const calendarViewHolder = document.getElementById("calendarViewHolder");

if (!now_indicator || !calendarViewHolder) {
    console.error("Element(s) not found");
    return;
}

// Calculate offset relative to #calendarViewHolder
let relativeOffsetTop = 0;
let currentElement = now_indicator;

// Loop through the offset chain until reaching the calendarViewHolder
while (currentElement && currentElement !== calendarViewHolder) {
    relativeOffsetTop += currentElement.offsetTop;
    currentElement = currentElement.offsetParent;
}

// Log the relative offset
console.log("scrolling to now indicator relative to calendarViewHolder:", relativeOffsetTop);

// Scroll the #calendarViewHolder to the relative position
calendarViewHolder.scrollTop = relativeOffsetTop - 400;


  }, 300);
  

}

// Renderiza o calendário com base na visão atual
function renderCalendar() {
    if (currentView === 'day') {
        renderDayView(currentDate);
    } else if (currentView === 'week') {
        renderWeekView(currentDate);
    } else if (currentView === 'month') {
        renderMonthView(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth());
    }
    updateViewLabel();
    get_posts_for_dates_interval();
    scrollToNow();
}

// Funções de Navegação
function goToToday() {
    currentDate = new Date();
    renderCalendar();
}

function goToPrevious() {
    if (currentView === 'day') {
        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() - 1);
    } else if (currentView === 'week') {
        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() - 7);
    } else if (currentView === 'month') {
        currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() - 1);
    }
    renderCalendar();
}

function goToNext() {
    if (currentView === 'day') {
        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() + 1);
    } else if (currentView === 'week') {
        currentDate.setDate(currentDate.getDate() + 7);
    } else if (currentView === 'month') {
        currentDate.setMonth(currentDate.getMonth() + 1);
    }
    renderCalendar();
}


function set_view_design_for_button(){
  //if current view is day, set week and month to opacity 0.75
  if (currentView === 'day'){
    document.getElementById("viewWeek").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewMonth").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewDay").style.opacity = "1";
  }else if (currentView === 'week'){
    document.getElementById("viewDay").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewMonth").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewWeek").style.opacity = "1";
  }else if (currentView === 'month'){
    document.getElementById("viewDay").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewWeek").style.opacity = "0.75";
    document.getElementById("viewMonth").style.opacity = "1";
  }


}

// Eventos dos Botões
document.getElementById("viewDay").addEventListener("click", () => {
    currentView = 'day';
    renderCalendar();
    set_view_design_for_button();
});
document.getElementById("viewWeek").addEventListener("click", () => {
    currentView = 'week';
    renderCalendar();
    set_view_design_for_button();
});
document.getElementById("viewMonth").addEventListener("click", () => {
    currentView = 'month';
    renderCalendar();
    set_view_design_for_button();
});
document.getElementById("today").addEventListener("click", goToToday);
document.getElementById("prev").addEventListener("click", goToPrevious);
document.getElementById("next").addEventListener("click", goToNext);


function get_latlng(){
  $.ajax({
        data: {
          get_latlng: true,
        },
        type: "POST",
        url: window.location.href
    }).done(function(data) {
      if (!data.lat || !data.lng){
        document.getElementById('gpsLatitude').value = "";
        document.getElementById('gpsLongitude').value = "";
        return;
      }

        const latlng = getRandomCoordinate(data.lat, data.lng, 2, 11);
        console.log("new latlng", latlng);
        document.getElementById('gpsLatitude').value = latlng.lat;
        document.getElementById('gpsLongitude').value = latlng.lng;
    });
}

function renderDayView(date) {
    const hours = Array.from({ length: 48 }, (_, i) => {
        const hour = Math.floor(i / 2);
        const minutes = i % 2 === 0 ? "00" : "30";
        return `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minutes}`;
    });

    const now = new Date();
    const currentDate = toLocalISOString(date).split("T")[0]; // Data no formato YYYY-MM-DD

    const dayOfWeek = date.toLocaleDateString("pt-BR", { weekday: "long" });

    let html = `<table class="day-view" data-date="${currentDate}">
        <thead>
            <tr>
                <th style="width: 60px; text-align: center;">Hora</th>
                <th style="text-align:center;">${dayOfWeek.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + dayOfWeek.slice(1)}</th>
            </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>`;

    hours.forEach((hour, index) => {
        const rowStartTime = new Date(date);
        rowStartTime.setHours(Math.floor(index / 2), (index % 2) * 30, 0, 0);

        const nextBlockTime = new Date(rowStartTime);
        nextBlockTime.setMinutes(rowStartTime.getMinutes() + 30);

        const is_time_in_this_cell = now >= rowStartTime && now < nextBlockTime;

        const isPast = now >= nextBlockTime && !is_time_in_this_cell;

        html += `
          <tr class="${isPast ? "date-past" : "date-future"}">
            <td style="width: 60px; text-align: center;">${hour}</td>
            <td data-date="${currentDate}" data-hour="${hour}"></td>
          </tr>`;
    });

    html += `</tbody></table>`;
    document.getElementById("calendarView").innerHTML = html;

    start_date_showing = currentDate;
    end_date_showing = currentDate;

    setTimeout(() => {
        renderNowIndicatorForDay();
    }, 300);


    attachCellEventHandlers();
}


function toLocalISOString(date) {
    // Obter o deslocamento de fuso horário em minutos e converter para milissegundos
    const timezoneOffset = date.getTimezoneOffset() * 60000;

    // Ajustar a data para o fuso horário local
    const localDate = new Date(date.getTime() - timezoneOffset);

    // Converter para o formato ISO sem alterar o horário
    return localDate.toISOString().slice(0, 19); // Remove a parte 'Z' que indica UTC
}



function isDatePast(date, now) {
    const dateString = toLocalISOString(date).split("T")[0];
    const nowString = toLocalISOString(now).split("T")[0];
    return dateString < nowString;
}



function renderWeekView(startDate) {
    const hours = Array.from({ length: 48 }, (_, i) => {
        const hour = Math.floor(i / 2);
        const minutes = i % 2 === 0 ? "00" : "30";
        return `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minutes}`;
    });

    const now = new Date();
    const daysOfWeek = Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => {
        const date = new Date(startDate);
        date.setDate(date.getDate() - date.getDay() + i);
        return {
            label:
                date.toLocaleDateString("pt-BR", { weekday: "short" }) +
                " " +
                date.toLocaleDateString("pt-BR", { day: "2-digit", month: "2-digit" }),
            date: toLocalISOString(date).split("T")[0],
        };
    });

    let html = `<table class="week-view">
        <thead>
            <tr>
                <th>Horário</th>
                ${daysOfWeek.map((day) => `<th data-date="${day.date}">${day.label}</th>`).join("")}
            </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>`;
    hours.forEach((hour) => {

        html += `<tr>
            <td>${hour}</td>
            ${daysOfWeek
                .map(
                    (day) =>
                        `<td data-date="${day.date}" data-hour="${hour}" class="${
                            (new Date(day.date + "T" + hour + ":00") < now)  ? "date-past" : "date-future"
                        }"></td>`
                )
                .join("")}
        </tr>`;

    });

    html += `</tbody></table>`;
    document.getElementById("calendarView").innerHTML = html;


        const date_past_all = document.querySelectorAll(".date-past");
      //remove date-past from last el
      if (date_past_all.length){

        date_past_all[date_past_all.length - 1].classList.remove("date-past");
      }

        start_date_showing = daysOfWeek[0].date;
        end_date_showing = daysOfWeek[6].date;

        setTimeout(() => {
          renderNowIndicatorForWeek();
    }, 300);

    
    attachCellEventHandlers();

}


function renderMonthView(year, month) {
  console.log("rendering month view", year, month);
    const date = new Date(year, month, 1);
    const daysInMonth = new Date(year, month + 1, 0).getDate();
    const firstDayIndex = date.getDay();
    const now = new Date();

    let html = `<table class="month-view">
        <thead style="height:40px;">
          <tr>
            ${[            translations["Dom"],
            translations["Seg"],
            translations["Ter"],
            translations["Qua"],
            translations["Qui"],
            translations["Sex"],
            translations["Sáb"]].map((day) => `<th>${day}</th>`).join("")}
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          <tr>`;

    for (let i = 0; i < firstDayIndex; i++) {
        html += `<td></td>`;
    }

    for (let day = 1; day <= daysInMonth; day++) {
        const currentDate = new Date(year, month, day);
        const currentDateString = toLocalISOString(currentDate).split("T")[0];
        const isPast = isDatePast(currentDate, now);

        html += `<td data-date="${currentDateString}" class="${isPast ? "date-past" : "date-future"}">${day}</td>`;

        if ((firstDayIndex + day) % 7 === 0) {
            html += `</tr><tr>`;
        }
    }

    const remainingCells = (firstDayIndex + daysInMonth) % 7;
    if (remainingCells !== 0) {
        for (let i = 0; i < 7 - remainingCells; i++) {
            html += `<td></td>`;
        }
    }

    html += `</tr></tbody></table>`;
    document.getElementById("calendarView").innerHTML = html;

    // Ajustar datas exibidas no intervalo do calendário
    start_date_showing = toLocalISOString(new Date(year, month, 1)).split("T")[0];
    end_date_showing = toLocalISOString(new Date(year, month, daysInMonth)).split("T")[0];

    attachCellEventHandlers();
}

document.getElementById("viewDay").addEventListener("click", () => renderDayView(new Date()));
document.getElementById("viewWeek").addEventListener("click", () => renderWeekView(new Date()));
document.getElementById("viewMonth").addEventListener("click", () => renderMonthView(currentDate.getFullYear(), currentDate.getMonth()));







function get_start_and_end_date() {
    return {
        start_date: start_date_showing,
        end_date: end_date_showing
    };
}




    function addHtmlToDate(dateStr, htmlContent) {
  var calendarEl = document.querySelector(`[data-date='${dateStr}']`);
  if (calendarEl) {
    calendarEl.innerHTML += htmlContent;
  }
}



function removeHtmlFromDate(dateStr) {
  var calendarEl = document.querySelector(`[data-date='${dateStr}']`);
  if (calendarEl) {
    calendarEl.innerHTML = ''; // Clear the content
  }
}

          state.post_now = true;

            $('input[name="birthday"]').val(start.format('DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm'));
        }

  
      });
  
      // Se post_now for true, define o valor "Agora" no input

      if (state.post_now) {
        $(this).val(translations["Agora"]);
      }
    });

        let currentDate = moment();
        if (currentDate.isSameOrAfter(selectedDate)) {
          $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setStartDate(moment());
          $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setEndDate(moment());
          $('input[name="birthday"]').val(translations["Agora"]);
          if (!state.post_now){
            state.post_now = true;
          }
        }
  
        //if minDate is lower than the current date, set the minDate to now
        if (minDate < currentDate) {
          $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').minDate = currentDate;
        }
  
    
    }, 1000);
  
    document.getElementById("reset-to-now").addEventListener("click", function() {
      $('input[name="birthday"]').val(translations["Agora"]);
      state.post_now = true;
      //set the date to now
      $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setStartDate(moment());
      $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setEndDate(moment());
  
    });

<script>

    // Variáveis globais para armazenar o estado e histórico
    let undoStack = [];
    let redoStack = [];
    let isUndoingRedoing = false;  // Flag to prevent adding states during undo/redo
    
    // Função para capturar o estado atual e adicionar ao histórico
    function saveState() {
        if (!isUndoingRedoing) {
            const currentState = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;
            undoStack.push(currentState);
    
            // Limpa o stack de redo, pois uma nova mudança invalida o redo anterior
            redoStack = [];
        }
    }
    
    // Função para desfazer a última mudança
    function undo() {
        if (undoStack.length > 0) {
            isUndoingRedoing = true;
            
            const currentState = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;
            redoStack.push(currentState);  // Salva o estado atual para o redo
            
            const previousState = undoStack.pop();  // Recupera o estado anterior
            document.getElementById('postDescription').value = previousState;
            
            isUndoingRedoing = false;
        }
    }
    
    // Função para refazer a última mudança desfeita
    function redo() {
        if (redoStack.length > 0) {
            isUndoingRedoing = true;
            
            const currentState = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;
            undoStack.push(currentState);  // Salva o estado atual para o undo
            
            const nextState = redoStack.pop();  // Recupera o estado para refazer
            document.getElementById('postDescription').value = nextState;
            
            isUndoingRedoing = false;
        }
    }
    
    
    
    
    
      document.getElementById('postDescription').addEventListener('input', function () {
        // Limit input to 1500 characters
        if (this.value.length > 1500) {
            this.value = this.value.substring(0, 1500);
        }
    
        const content_length = this.value.length;
        document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = content_length;
    
        if (!content_length){
          //disable optimize-text
          document.getElementById('optimize-text').disabled = true;
        }else{
          //enable optimize-text
          document.getElementById('optimize-text').disabled = false;
        }
      });
    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
      // Function to open the suggestion box
    function open_image_suggestion_box() {
        const suggestionBox = document.getElementById('suggestion-box');
        suggestionBox.style.display = 'flex';
    
    
    }
    
    // Function to close the suggestion box
    function close_image_suggestion_box() {
        const suggestionBox = document.getElementById('suggestion-box');
        suggestionBox.style.display = 'none';
    }
    
    // Make the suggestion box draggable
    //dragElement(document.getElementById('suggestion-box'));
    
    function dragElement(el) {
        var pos1 = 0, pos2 = 0, pos3 = 0, pos4 = 0;
        if (document.getElementById(el.id + "header")) {
            // If present, the header is where you move the DIV from:
            document.getElementById(el.id + "header").onmousedown = dragMouseDown;
        } else {
            // Otherwise, move the DIV from anywhere inside the DIV:
            el.onmousedown = dragMouseDown;
        }
    
        function dragMouseDown(e) {
            e = e || window.event;
            e.preventDefault();
            // Get the mouse cursor position at startup:
            pos3 = e.clientX;
            pos4 = e.clientY;
            document.onmouseup = closeDragElement;
            // Call a function whenever the cursor moves:
            document.onmousemove = elementDrag;
        }
    
        function elementDrag(e) {
            e = e || window.event;
            e.preventDefault();
            // Calculate the new cursor position:
            pos1 = pos3 - e.clientX;
            pos2 = pos4 - e.clientY;
            pos3 = e.clientX;
            pos4 = e.clientY;
            // Set the element's new position:
            el.style.top = (el.offsetTop - pos2) + "px";
            el.style.left = (el.offsetLeft - pos1) + "px";
        }
    
        function closeDragElement() {
            // Stop moving when mouse button is released:
            document.onmouseup = null;
            document.onmousemove = null;
        }
    }
    
    </script>

<script>


    function select_timezone(selected_el){
  
  
      document.querySelectorAll("#timezone-list a").forEach(function(el){
        el.style.fontWeight = "normal";
      });
  
      selected_el.style.fontWeight = "bold";
  
    }
    
    var selected_timezone_for_location = "local";
    var selected_timezone_offset = null;

    console.log("init")
    console.log(moment); // Deve mostrar um objeto com funções
console.log(moment.tz); // Deve mostrar uma função, não "undefined"
console.log(moment.tz.names); // Deve mostrar um array de timezones
console.log("end")

  
    // Lista de timezones disponíveis no Moment-Timezone
    const timezones = moment.tz.names();
    
    // Elemento onde serão injetadas as opções
    const timezoneList = document.getElementById('timezone-list');
    
    // Função para renderizar o dropdown com as opções de timezone
    function renderTimezones(filteredTimezones) {
    timezoneList.innerHTML = ''; // Limpa a lista de timezones
    
    // Primeira opção fixa: "Usar fuso local"
    const localOption = document.createElement('a');
    localOption.className = 'dropdown-item';
    localOption.href = '#';
    localOption.textContent = 'Usar fuso local';
    localOption.style.borderBottom = '1px solid #ccc';
  
  
    localOption.onclick = function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
  
        select_timezone(this);
  
        selected_timezone_for_location = "local";
        selected_timezone_offset = moment.tz.guess();
  
        const localTimezone = moment.tz.guess();
        const localOffset = moment.tz(localTimezone).format('Z');
        console.log(`Using Local Timezone: ${localTimezone}`);
        console.log(`Local GMT Offset: ${localOffset}`);
    
        document.getElementById('selected-timezone').innerText = 'Local';
  
        save_timezone_for_location();
    
    
    };
    timezoneList.appendChild(localOption);
    // Renderizando timezones filtrados
    filteredTimezones.forEach((zone) => {
        const option = document.createElement('a');
        option.className = 'dropdown-item';
        option.href = '#';
        option.textContent = zone;
        option.style.borderBottom = '1px solid #ccc';
        option.onclick = function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
  
            select_timezone(this);
            const offset = moment.tz(zone).format('Z');
            console.log(`Selected Timezone: ${zone}`);
            console.log(`GMT Offset: ${offset}`);
  
            selected_timezone_for_location = zone;
            selected_timezone_offset = offset;
  
    
            document.getElementById('selected-timezone').innerText = zone + ' (' + offset + ')';
  
            save_timezone_for_location();
        };
        timezoneList.appendChild(option);
    });
    }
    
    // Inicialmente renderiza todos os timezones
    renderTimezones(timezones);
    
    // Filtro de busca
    const timezoneSearch = document.getElementById('timezone-search');
    timezoneSearch.addEventListener('input', function() {
    const searchTerm = this.value.toLowerCase().replace('_', '').replace(' ', ''); // Remover underscores e normalizar texto
    const filteredTimezones = timezones.filter(zone =>
        zone.toLowerCase().replace('_', '').includes(searchTerm)
    );
    renderTimezones(filteredTimezones); // Re-renderiza a lista com base no filtro
  
    set_timezone(selected_timezone_for_location);
    });
    
    // Prevenir o fechamento do dropdown ao selecionar uma opção
    // $('.dropdown-menu').on('click', function(e) {
    // e.stopPropagation();
    // });
  </script>

          <button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close">
            <span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>

        <script>


          function getExifData() {
    return {
        metadataAdded: document.querySelector("#addMetadata").checked,
        title: document.querySelector("#title").value,
        description: document.querySelector("#description").value,
        keywords: document.querySelector("#keywords").value.replaceAll(",", ";"),
        gpsLatitude: document.querySelector("#gpsLatitude").value,
        gpsLongitude: document.querySelector("#gpsLongitude").value,
        fileName: document.querySelector("#fileName").value,
    };
}


document.getElementById("addMetadata").addEventListener("change", function() {
    const metadataFields = document.querySelectorAll("#metaHolder input[type='text']");
    metadataFields.forEach(field => {
        field.disabled = !this.checked;
    });
});
        

function check_filename_metadata(el){
  let fileName = el.value;
    
    // Verifica se existe um ponto no nome do arquivo
    if (fileName.includes('.')) {
        // Remove tudo após o último ponto, incluindo o ponto
        fileName = fileName.substring(0, fileName.lastIndexOf('.'));
    }
    
    fileName = fileName.replaceAll("_", "-");

    // Substitui caracteres com acentos por suas versões normais
    fileName = fileName.normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, "");
    
    // Remove todos os caracteres não alfanuméricos, exceto espaços, hífens e caracteres latinos
    fileName = fileName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9\s-çáéíóúãõâêîôûäëïöü]/g, "");
    
    // Substitui espaços consecutivos ou múltiplos hífens por um único hífen
    fileName = fileName.replace(/\s+/g, '-').replace(/--+/g, "-");
    
    // Atualiza o valor do campo
    el.value = fileName;


}

document.getElementById("fileName").addEventListener("focusout", function() {
  check_filename_metadata(this);
});


document.getElementById("keywords").addEventListener("focusout", function() {
    const keywords = this.value;
    // Remove todos os espaços em branco no início e no final da string
    let formattedKeywords = keywords.trim();

    formattedKeywords = formattedKeywords.replaceAll("; ", ";").replaceAll(" ;", ";").replaceAll(" ; ", ";");

    // Substitui todos os espaços duplos ou mais por um único espaço
    this.value = formattedKeywords.replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ');
});


document.getElementById("gpsLatitude").addEventListener("focusout", function() {
    const latitude = this.value;
    //remove all non numeric characters, excluding the dot and minus sign
    const formattedLatitude = latitude.replace(/[^0-9.-]/g, '');
    this.value = formattedLatitude;
});

document.getElementById("gpsLongitude").addEventListener("focusout", function() {
    const longitude = this.value;
    //remove all non numeric characters, excluding the dot and minus sign
    const formattedLongitude = longitude.replace(/[^0-9.-]/g, '');
    this.value = formattedLongitude;
});







        </script>
