  <script>

    // Global variables - IMPORTANT: Must be declared BEFORE any external scripts use them
    window.selected_images = [];  // Force global scope
    var validationErrors = [];
    

    // Image validation configuration
    const IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG = {
        MIN_WIDTH: 250,
        MIN_HEIGHT: 250,
        MIN_FILE_SIZE: 10240, // 10KB in bytes
        MAX_FILE_SIZE: 20 * 1024 * 1024, // 20MB in bytes
        MAX_IMAGES: 1, // APENAS 1 IMAGEM POR POST
        SUPPORTED_FORMATS: ['image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/png']
    };

    // Enhanced format validation using multiple methods
    function validateImageFormat(file) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = function(e) {
                const arr = new Uint8Array(e.target.result);
                
                // Check for JPEG magic bytes (multiple variations)
                const isJPEG = (
                    (arr[0] === 0xFF && arr[1] === 0xD8 && arr[2] === 0xFF && arr[3] === 0xE0) || // JFIF
                    (arr[0] === 0xFF && arr[1] === 0xD8 && arr[2] === 0xFF && arr[3] === 0xE1) || // EXIF
                    (arr[0] === 0xFF && arr[1] === 0xD8 && arr[2] === 0xFF && arr[3] === 0xDB) || // Standard JPEG
                    (arr[0] === 0xFF && arr[1] === 0xD8 && arr[2] === 0xFF && arr[3] === 0xEE)    // Canon
                );
                
                // Check for PNG magic bytes
                const isPNG = (
                    arr[0] === 0x89 && arr[1] === 0x50 && arr[2] === 0x4E && arr[3] === 0x47 &&
                    arr[4] === 0x0D && arr[5] === 0x0A && arr[6] === 0x1A && arr[7] === 0x0A
                );
                
                // Check for WEBP (must be rejected)
                const isWEBP = (
                    arr[0] === 0x52 && arr[1] === 0x49 && arr[2] === 0x46 && arr[3] === 0x46 &&
                    arr[8] === 0x57 && arr[9] === 0x45 && arr[10] === 0x42 && arr[11] === 0x50
                );
                
                // Check for GIF (must be rejected)  
                const isGIF = (
                    (arr[0] === 0x47 && arr[1] === 0x49 && arr[2] === 0x46 && arr[3] === 0x38 && arr[4] === 0x37 && arr[5] === 0x61) || // GIF87a
                    (arr[0] === 0x47 && arr[1] === 0x49 && arr[2] === 0x46 && arr[3] === 0x38 && arr[4] === 0x39 && arr[5] === 0x61)    // GIF89a
                );
                
                // Check for BMP (must be rejected)
                const isBMP = (arr[0] === 0x42 && arr[1] === 0x4D);
                
                // Check for TIFF (must be rejected)
                const isTIFF = (
                    (arr[0] === 0x49 && arr[1] === 0x49 && arr[2] === 0x2A && arr[3] === 0x00) || // Little-endian
                    (arr[0] === 0x4D && arr[1] === 0x4D && arr[2] === 0x00 && arr[3] === 0x2A)    // Big-endian
                );

                console.log('🔍 File format validation:', {
                    fileName: file.name,
                    mimeType: file.type,
                    magicBytes: Array.from(arr.slice(0, 12)).map(b => '0x' + b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join(' '),
                    isJPEG, isPNG, isWEBP, isGIF, isBMP, isTIFF
                });
                
                if (isWEBP) {
                    console.log('🚫 WEBP format detected - REJECTING completely');
                    reject('❌ Formato WEBP detectado! Este formato foi renomeado incorretamente. Use apenas JPG ou PNG originais.');
                    return; // Explicit return to make sure nothing else executes
                } else if (isGIF) {
                    console.log('🚫 GIF format detected - REJECTING completely');
                    reject('❌ Formato GIF detectado! Este formato não é suportado. Use apenas JPG ou PNG.');
                    return;
                } else if (isBMP) {
                    console.log('🚫 BMP format detected - REJECTING completely');
                    reject('❌ Formato BMP detectado! Este formato não é suportado. Use apenas JPG ou PNG.');  
                    return;
                } else if (isTIFF) {
                    console.log('🚫 TIFF format detected - REJECTING completely');
                    reject('❌ Formato TIFF detectado! Este formato não é suportado. Use apenas JPG ou PNG.');
                    return;
                } else if (!isJPEG && !isPNG) {
                    console.log('🚫 Unknown format detected - REJECTING completely');
                    reject('❌ Formato de imagem não reconhecido ou corrompido. Use apenas JPG ou PNG originais.');
                    return;
                } else {
                    resolve(true);
                }
            };
            reader.readAsArrayBuffer(file.slice(0, 20)); // Read more bytes for better detection
        });
    }

    function validateImageDimensions(file) {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const img = new Image();
            img.onload = function() {
                // Additional validation: try to draw on canvas to ensure it's a valid image
                const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
                
                try {
                    canvas.width = img.width;
                    canvas.height = img.height;
                    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
                    
                    // Try to get image data to ensure it's truly valid
                    const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, Math.min(10, img.width), Math.min(10, img.height));
                    
                    if (!imageData || imageData.data.length === 0) {
                        reject('❌ Arquivo corrompido ou formato inválido disfarçado.');
                        return;
                    }
                    
                } catch (error) {
                    reject('❌ Formato de imagem inválido ou corrompido. O arquivo pode ter sido renomeado incorretamente.');
                    return;
                }
                
                if (img.width < IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_WIDTH || img.height < IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_HEIGHT) {
                    reject(`❌ Imagem muito pequena. Dimensões: ${img.width}px/${img.height}px (mínimo: ${IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_WIDTH}px/${IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_HEIGHT}px largura/altura).`);
                } else {
                    resolve({ width: img.width, height: img.height });
                }
            };
            img.onerror = () => {
                reject('❌ Não foi possível carregar a imagem. Formato inválido ou arquivo corrompido.');
            };
            img.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);
        });
    }

    function validateImageSize(file) {
        if (file.size < IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_FILE_SIZE) {
            return {
                valid: false,
                error: `❌ Arquivo muito pequeno. Tamanho: ${file.size}B (mínimo: ${IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MIN_FILE_SIZE}B).`
            };
        }
        if (file.size > IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
            return {
                valid: false,
                error: `❌ Arquivo muito grande. Tamanho: ${(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)}MB (máximo: ${IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MAX_FILE_SIZE / 1024 / 1024}MB).`
            };
        }
        return { valid: true };
    }

    function showValidationError(message, isWarning = false) {
        const alertClass = isWarning ? 'alert-warning' : 'alert-danger';
        const iconClass = isWarning ? 'fa-exclamation-triangle' : 'fa-times-circle';
        
        // Remove previous errors only when showing a new one
        const existingAlerts = document.querySelectorAll('.alert');
        existingAlerts.forEach(alert => alert.remove());
        
        const errorHtml = `
            <div class="alert ${alertClass} alert-dismissible fade show validation-alert" role="alert" style="margin: 10px 0; border-radius: 8px;">
                <i class="fas ${iconClass}" style="margin-right: 8px;"></i>
                <strong>${isWarning ? 'Atenção:' : 'Erro:'}</strong> ${message}
                <button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="alert" aria-label="Close">
                    <span aria-hidden="true">&times;</span>
                </button>
            </div>
        `;
        
        // Insert error above the upload area
        const uploadArea = document.getElementById('drop-area');
        uploadArea.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin', errorHtml);
        
        // NO AUTO-REMOVE - User must close manually or upload new image
    }
    
    function clearValidationErrors() {
        const existingAlerts = document.querySelectorAll('.validation-alert, .alert');
        existingAlerts.forEach(alert => alert.remove());
    }

    async function validateAndAddImage(file) {
        console.log('📊 Current selected_images count BEFORE clearing:', window.selected_images ? window.selected_images.length : 0);
        
        // FIRST: Clear all existing image data before any validation
        clearAllImageData();
        
        try {
            // Check file size first (fastest check)
            const sizeValidation = validateImageSize(file);
            if (!sizeValidation.valid) {
                showValidationError(sizeValidation.error);
                return false;
            }

            // Check format by magic bytes - THIS CAN THROW EXCEPTION
            try {
                await validateImageFormat(file);
            } catch (formatError) {
                console.log('🛑 STOPPING validation process - returning false');
                console.log('📊 Current selected_images count AFTER format error:', window.selected_images ? window.selected_images.length : 0);
                showValidationError(formatError);
                return false; // STOP HERE - DO NOT CONTINUE
            }

            // Check dimensions - THIS CAN ALSO THROW EXCEPTION
            let dimensions;
            try {
                dimensions = await validateImageDimensions(file);
            } catch (dimensionError) {
                showValidationError(dimensionError);
                return false; // STOP HERE - DO NOT CONTINUE
            }

            // Note: Image clearing is now done at the start of this function

            // If ALL validations pass, convert to base64 and add to array
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(e) {
                    const imageData = {
                        name: file.name,
                        size: file.size,
                        type: file.type,
                        url: e.target.result,
                        dimensions: dimensions,
                        validated: true
                    };
                    
                    // Use window.selected_images to ensure global scope
                    window.selected_images.push(imageData);
                    
                    // Clear any previous validation errors when image is successfully added
                    clearValidationErrors();
                    
                    updateImagePreview();
                    // Image successfully added
                    resolve(true);
                };
                reader.onerror = function(error) {
                    showValidationError('❌ Erro ao processar o arquivo.');
                    // DO NOT add to any array on error
                    resolve(false);
                };
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            });

        } catch (error) {
            showValidationError('❌ Erro inesperado ao validar a imagem.');
            console.log('🛑 RETURNING FALSE due to unexpected error');
            return false;
        }
    }

    function updateImagePreview() {
        console.trace('🔄 Call stack:');
        
        // Always use manual carousel update for validated images to avoid conflicts
        manuallyUpdateCarousel();
        
        // Update button states
        updatePublishButtonStates();
    }
    
    function manuallyUpdateCarousel() {
        updateCarouselPreview();
        updateUploadArea();
    }
    
    function updateCarouselPreview() {
        const carouselContainer = document.getElementById('carousel-images');
        if (!carouselContainer) {
            return;
        }
        
        
        // Clear existing images
        carouselContainer.innerHTML = '';
        
        
        if (window.selected_images.length > 0) {
            // Force containers to be visible when there are images
            carouselContainer.style.setProperty('display', 'flex', 'important');
            
            const carouselContainerParent = document.getElementById('carousel-container');
            if (carouselContainerParent) {
                carouselContainerParent.style.setProperty('display', 'block', 'important');
            }
            
            // HIDE ONLY the megaphone icon when there are images, keep the text section
            const megaphoneIcon = document.getElementById('previewIconMegaphone');
            if (megaphoneIcon) {
                megaphoneIcon.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
            }
        } else {
            // Force containers to be hidden when no images
            carouselContainer.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
            
            const carouselContainerParent = document.getElementById('carousel-container');
            if (carouselContainerParent) {
                carouselContainerParent.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
            }
            
            // Check if there's text in the post
            const postDescription = document.getElementById('postDescription');
            const hasText = postDescription && postDescription.value.trim().length > 0;
            
            // Only show megaphone if there's NO text either
            const megaphoneIcon = document.getElementById('previewIconMegaphone');
            if (megaphoneIcon) {
                if (hasText) {
                    // If there's text but no images, hide the megaphone
                    megaphoneIcon.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
                } else {
                    // Only show megaphone when there's no text AND no images
                    megaphoneIcon.style.setProperty('display', 'block', 'important');
                }
            }
            
            return; // Don't add any images
        }
        
        // Add new images to preview area
        window.selected_images.forEach((imageData, index) => {
            
            const imgDiv = document.createElement('div');
            imgDiv.style.cssText = 'position: relative; display: block; margin: 5px; width: 100%;';
            
            const img = document.createElement('img');
            img.src = imageData.url;
            img.style.cssText = 'width: 100%; height: auto; border-radius: 8px; display: block;';
            img.alt = imageData.name || 'Uploaded image';
            
            // Hide carousel when image fails to load in main system
            img.onerror = function() {
                img.style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById("images-selected").style.display = "none";
                document.getElementById("carousel-images").style.display = "none";
                document.querySelectorAll('.img-area-container').forEach(function (el) {
                    el.style.display = 'flex';
                });
            };
            
            imgDiv.appendChild(img);
            carouselContainer.appendChild(imgDiv);
        });
        
    }
    
    function updateUploadArea() {
        const uploadContainer = document.getElementById('images-selected');
        const imgAreaContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.img-area-container');
        
        
        if (window.selected_images.length > 0) {
            // Hide upload buttons and show selected images area
            imgAreaContainers.forEach(container => {
                container.style.display = 'none';
            });
            
            if (uploadContainer) {
                uploadContainer.style.display = 'flex';
                uploadContainer.innerHTML = '';
                
                // Add images to upload area
                window.selected_images.forEach((imageData, index) => {
                    const imgDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    imgDiv.style.cssText = 'position: relative; margin: 5px;';
                    
                    const img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.src = imageData.url;
                    img.style.cssText = 'max-width: 120px; max-height: 80px; border-radius: 5px; border: 1px solid #ccc; cursor: pointer;';
                    img.alt = imageData.name || 'Uploaded image';
                    
                    // Hide carousel when image fails to load in main system
                    img.onerror = function() {
                        img.style.display = 'none';
                        document.getElementById("images-selected").style.display = "none";
                        document.getElementById("carousel-images").style.display = "none";
                        document.querySelectorAll('.img-area-container').forEach(function (el) {
                            el.style.display = 'flex';
                        });
                    };
                    
                    // Add click event to open crop modal
                    img.onclick = function() {
                        const currentIndex = index; // Capture current index
                        
                        // Prepare image data with required properties for crop modal
                        const imageForCrop = {
                            ...window.selected_images[currentIndex],
                            size: window.selected_images[currentIndex].dimensions ? 
                                  `${window.selected_images[currentIndex].dimensions.width}x${window.selected_images[currentIndex].dimensions.height}` : 
                                  '1080x1080', // Default size if not available
                            title: window.selected_images[currentIndex].name || 'image',
                            id: currentIndex
                        };
                        
                        // Save original recreate_images_selected function temporarily
                        const originalRecreateFunction = window.recreate_images_selected;
                        
                        // Override recreate_images_selected to update our array instead
                        window.recreate_images_selected = function() {
                            if (selected_images_search.length > 0 && selected_images_search[0]) {
                                // Update window.selected_images with the cropped version
                                window.selected_images[currentIndex] = {
                                    ...window.selected_images[currentIndex],
                                    url: selected_images_search[0].url,
                                    bkpSrc: selected_images_search[0].bkpSrc || window.selected_images[currentIndex].url
                                };
                                // Update display without calling the search version
                                updateImagePreview();
                            }
                        };
                        
                        // Copy image to selected_images_search for crop modal to work
                        selected_images_search = [imageForCrop];
                        global_crop_index = 0;
                        file_title_global = imageForCrop.name || imageForCrop.title || 'image';
                        
                        // Open modal
                        openCropModal(0);
                        
                        // Restore original function after modal is fully hidden
                        $('#cropModal').off('hidden.bs.modal.restore').on('hidden.bs.modal.restore', function() {
                            window.recreate_images_selected = originalRecreateFunction;
                        });
                    };
                    
                    // Add remove button
                    const removeBtn = document.createElement('button');
                    removeBtn.innerHTML = '×';
                    removeBtn.style.cssText = 'position: absolute; top: -5px; right: -5px; width: 18px; height: 18px; border-radius: 50%; background: #dc3545; color: white; border: none; cursor: pointer; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1; z-index: 10;';
                    removeBtn.onclick = (e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation(); // Prevent triggering image click
                        removeImage(index);
                    };
                    
                    imgDiv.appendChild(img);
                    imgDiv.appendChild(removeBtn);
                    uploadContainer.appendChild(imgDiv);
                });
            }
        } else {
            // Show upload buttons and hide selected images area
            imgAreaContainers.forEach(container => {
                container.style.display = 'flex';
            });
            
            if (uploadContainer) {
                uploadContainer.style.display = 'none';
                uploadContainer.innerHTML = '';
            }
        }
    }
    
    function clearAllImageData() {
        console.log('🧹 CLEARING ALL IMAGE DATA - resetting to zero state');
        
        // Clear ALL image-related arrays completely
        window.selected_images = [];
        
        // Clear uploaded_images from image_search.js
        if (typeof uploaded_images !== 'undefined') {
            uploaded_images.length = 0; // Clear array contents
        }
        
        // Clear selected_images_search from image_search.js  
        if (typeof selected_images_search !== 'undefined') {
            selected_images_search.length = 0; // Clear array contents
        }
        
        // Clear any other image-related global variables
        if (typeof global_crop_index !== 'undefined') {
            global_crop_index = -1;
        }
        
        // Clear validation errors array
        if (typeof validationErrors !== 'undefined') {
            validationErrors.length = 0;
        }
        
        // Clear any validation errors from UI
        clearValidationErrors();
        
        // Reset file input
        const uploadInput = document.getElementById('upload-media-input');
        if (uploadInput) {
            uploadInput.value = '';
        }
        
        // Clear and FORCEFULLY HIDE all image containers
        const carouselImages = document.getElementById('carousel-images');
        if (carouselImages) {
            carouselImages.innerHTML = '';
            carouselImages.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important'); // FORCE HIDE carousel
        }
        
        const carouselContainer = document.getElementById('carousel-container');
        if (carouselContainer) {
            carouselContainer.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important'); // FORCE HIDE container
        }
        
        const imagesSelected = document.getElementById('images-selected');
        if (imagesSelected) {
            imagesSelected.innerHTML = '';
            imagesSelected.style.display = 'none';
        }
        
        // Update UI to show upload buttons again
        updateImagePreview();
        
    }

    function removeImage(index) {
        clearAllImageData();
    }
    
    function updatePublishButtonStates() {
        
        const description = document.getElementById('postDescription') ? 
                          document.getElementById('postDescription').value.trim() : '';
        const hasValidImages = window.selected_images && 
                              window.selected_images.length > 0 && 
                              window.selected_images.every(img => img.validated === true);
        
        const canPublish = description.length > 0 || hasValidImages;
        
        // Update publish/schedule button
        const publishButton = document.getElementById('publish_now');
        if (publishButton) {
            if (!canPublish) {
                publishButton.disabled = true;
                publishButton.style.opacity = '0.5';
                publishButton.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
                publishButton.title = 'Adicione texto ou imagem válida para publicar';
            } else {
                publishButton.disabled = false;
                publishButton.style.opacity = '1';
                publishButton.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                publishButton.title = '';
            }
        }
        
        // Button state updated
    }

    function validateBeforePublish() {
        const description = document.getElementById('postDescription').value.trim();
        const hasValidImages = window.selected_images && window.selected_images.length > 0 && 
                               window.selected_images.every(img => img.validated === true);
        const hasImages = window.selected_images && window.selected_images.length > 0;
        
        // Pre-publish validation
        
        // CRITICAL: Must have text OR valid images
        if (!description && !hasValidImages) {
            showValidationError('❌ A publicação deve ter pelo menos uma imagem válida ou um texto.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // If has images but they're invalid
        if (hasImages && !hasValidImages) {
            const invalidImages = window.selected_images.filter(img => !img.validated);
            showValidationError('❌ Existem imagens inválidas. Remova todas as imagens e adicione novamente.');
            
            // Clear invalid images
            window.selected_images = [];
            updateImagePreview();
            return false;
        }
        
        // Double-check if there are too many images
        if (window.selected_images && window.selected_images.length > IMAGE_VALIDATION_CONFIG.MAX_IMAGES) {
            showValidationError('❌ Apenas 1 imagem por post é permitida.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Validate event and offer specific fields
        if (post_type === "event") {
            if (!validateEventFields()) {
                return false;
            }
        } else if (post_type === "offer") {
            if (!validateOfferFields()) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        
        // Pre-publish validation passed
        return true;
    }
    
    function validateEventFields() {
        const startDate = $('#eventStartDate').val();
        const endDate = $('#eventEndDate').val();
        const startTime = $('#eventStartHour').val();
        const endTime = $('#eventEndHour').val();
        
        // Check required dates with specific messages
        if (!startDate && !endDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para eventos, a data de início e a data de fim são obrigatórias.');
            return false;
        } else if (!startDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para eventos, a data de início é obrigatória.');
            return false;
        } else if (!endDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para eventos, a data de fim é obrigatória.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check if end date is in the past
        const today = new Date();
        today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        const eventEndDate = new Date(endDate);
        
        if (eventEndDate < today) {
            showValidationError('❌ A data de fim do evento não pode ser no passado.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check if dates are within 1 year
        const oneYearFromNow = new Date();
        oneYearFromNow.setFullYear(oneYearFromNow.getFullYear() + 1);
        const eventStartDate = new Date(startDate);
        
        if (eventStartDate > oneYearFromNow || eventEndDate > oneYearFromNow) {
            showValidationError('❌ As datas do evento devem estar dentro de 1 ano.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check end date is after start date
        if (eventEndDate < eventStartDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ A data de fim deve ser posterior à data de início.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // If start time is provided, end time must also be provided
        if (startTime && !endTime) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para eventos, se o horário de início for fornecido, o horário de fim também deve ser fornecido.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // If end time is provided, start time must also be provided
        if (endTime && !startTime) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para eventos, se o horário de fim for fornecido, o horário de início também deve ser fornecido.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // If on same day, end time must be after start time
        if (startDate === endDate && startTime && endTime && endTime <= startTime) {
            showValidationError('❌ O horário de fim deve ser posterior ao horário de início no mesmo dia.');
            return false;
        }
        
        return true;
    }
    
    function validateOfferFields() {
        const startDate = $('#offerStartDate').val();
        const endDate = $('#offerEndDate').val();
        
        // Check required dates with specific messages
        if (!startDate && !endDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para ofertas, a data de início e a data de fim são obrigatórias.');
            return false;
        } else if (!startDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para ofertas, a data de início é obrigatória.');
            return false;
        } else if (!endDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ Para ofertas, a data de fim é obrigatória.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check if end date is in the past
        const today = new Date();
        today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
        const offerEndDate = new Date(endDate);
        
        if (offerEndDate < today) {
            showValidationError('❌ A data de fim da oferta não pode ser no passado.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check if dates are within 1 year
        const oneYearFromNow = new Date();
        oneYearFromNow.setFullYear(oneYearFromNow.getFullYear() + 1);
        const offerStartDate = new Date(startDate);
        
        if (offerStartDate > oneYearFromNow || offerEndDate > oneYearFromNow) {
            showValidationError('❌ As datas da oferta devem estar dentro de 1 ano.');
            return false;
        }
        
        // Check end date is after start date
        if (offerEndDate < offerStartDate) {
            showValidationError('❌ A data de fim deve ser posterior à data de início.');
            return false;
        }
        
        return true;
    }

    // Função para converter string de data (yyyy-mm-dd) em objeto Date
function convertToDateObject(dateString) {
  const [year, month, day] = dateString.split('-').map(Number);
  return {
    year: year,
    month: month, // JavaScript Date usa 0-index para meses, mas aqui usamos 1-index
    day: day
  };
}

// Função para criar objeto TimeOfDay com valores padrão (00:00:00)
function createDefaultTimeOfDay() {
  return {
    hours: 0,
    minutes: 0,
    seconds: 0,
    nanos: 0
  };
}

// Função para converter string de hora (HH:mm) em objeto TimeOfDay
function convertToTimeOfDayObject(timeString) {
  const [hours, minutes] = timeString.split(':').map(Number);
  return {
    hours: hours,
    minutes: minutes,
    seconds: 0,
    nanos: 0
  };
}


// Função para redimensionar a imagem mantendo o aspect ratio
function createThumbnail(base64Image, maxHeight) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const img = new Image();
        img.src = base64Image;
        img.onload = function () {
            const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            
            // Calcula o fator de escala para manter a proporção
            const scaleFactor = maxHeight / img.height;
            const newWidth = img.width * scaleFactor;
            const newHeight = maxHeight;

            // Define as dimensões do canvas
            canvas.width = newWidth;
            canvas.height = newHeight;

            // Desenha a imagem redimensionada no canvas
            ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, newWidth, newHeight);

            // Converte o canvas de volta para base64 jpeg
            const thumbnailBase64 = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg');
            resolve(thumbnailBase64); // Retorna a imagem redimensionada
        };

        img.onerror = reject; // Caso ocorra um erro
    });
}





var post_offer_info = {
    title: "",
    description: "",
    start_date: "",
    end_date: "",
    coupom_code: "",
    coupom_redeem_url: "",
    terms_and_conditions: ""
  }

    title: "",
    description: "",
    start_date: "",
    end_date: "",
    start_hour: "",
    end_hour: "",
  }


  function fill_post_offer_info(){

    const startDateInput = $('#offerStartDate').val();
    const endDateInput = $('#offerEndDate').val();


    post_offer_info.title = document.getElementById('postTitleOptional').value;
    post_offer_info.description = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;
    post_offer_info.start_date = startDateInput ? convertToDateObject(startDateInput) : null;
    post_offer_info.end_date = endDateInput ? convertToDateObject(endDateInput) : null;
    post_offer_info.coupom_code = document.getElementById('offerCoupomCode').value;
    post_offer_info.coupom_redeem_url = document.getElementById('offerCoupomRedeemUrl').value;
    post_offer_info.terms_and_conditions = document.getElementById('offerTermsAndConditions').value;
  }

  function fill_post_event_info(){
    // Capturar valores dos inputs
const startDateInput = $('#eventStartDate').val();
const endDateInput = $('#eventEndDate').val();
const startHourInput = $('#eventStartHour').val();
const endHourInput = $('#eventEndHour').val();


    post_event_info.title = document.getElementById('postTitleOptional').value;
    post_event_info.description = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;

    // Criar os objetos no formato desejado
post_event_info.start_date = startDateInput ? convertToDateObject(startDateInput) : null;
post_event_info.end_date = endDateInput ? convertToDateObject(endDateInput) : null;
post_event_info.start_hour = startHourInput ? convertToTimeOfDayObject(startHourInput) : null;
post_event_info.end_hour = endHourInput ? convertToTimeOfDayObject(endHourInput) : null;

  }



  function isValidUrl(url) {
    try {
        // Normaliza a URL substituindo barras invertidas por barras normais
        const normalizedUrl = url.replace(/\\+/g, '/');
        
        // Expressão regular para validar URLs
        const urlPattern = /^(https?:\/\/)?([a-zA-Z0-9.-]+)\.[a-zA-Z]{2,}(:\d+)?(\/.*)?$/;
        
        return urlPattern.test(normalizedUrl);
    } catch (e) {
        return false;
    }
}





  function verify_needed_fields_offer(){
    // start date and end date 
    console.log(post_offer_info.start_date);
    console.log(post_offer_info.end_date);
    if (!post_offer_info.start_date || !post_offer_info.end_date){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira a data de início e término da oferta.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error A");
      return false;
    }else{
      // start date be after or equal to today
      const startDate = new Date(post_offer_info.start_date.year, post_offer_info.start_date.month - 1, post_offer_info.start_date.day);
      const currentDate = new Date();


      // Zerar horas, minutos, segundos e milissegundos
      startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      currentDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);


      if (startDate < currentDate) {
        //modal error
        document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
        document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "A data de início da oferta deve ser igual ou posterior à data atual.";
        $('#post-return').modal('show');
        console.log("error B");
        return false;
      }


      // end date be after start date
      const endDate = new Date(post_offer_info.end_date.year, post_offer_info.end_date.month - 1, post_offer_info.end_date.day);
      if (endDate < startDate) {
        //modal error
        document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
        document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "A data de término da oferta deve ser igual ou posterior à data de início.";
        $('#post-return').modal('show');
        console.log("error C");
        return false;
      }


    }


    //title
    if (!post_offer_info.title){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira um título para a oferta.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error B");
      return false;
    }


    // title must be at most 58 characters
    if (post_offer_info.title.length > 58){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "O título da oferta deve ter no máximo 58 caracteres.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error C");
      return false;
    }


    return true;
  }

  function verify_needed_fields_event(){

    // start date and end date 
    console.log(post_event_info.start_date);
    console.log(post_event_info.end_date);
    if (!post_event_info.start_date || !post_event_info.end_date){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira a data de início e término do evento.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error A");
      return false;
    }else{
      // start date be after or equal to today
      const startDate = new Date(post_event_info.start_date.year, post_event_info.start_date.month - 1, post_event_info.start_date.day);
      const currentDate = new Date();


      // Zerar horas, minutos, segundos e milissegundos
      startDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      currentDate.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

      if (startDate < currentDate) {
        //modal error
        document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
        document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "A data de início do evento deve ser igual ou posterior à data atual.";
        $('#post-return').modal('show');
        console.log("error B");
        return false;
      }

      // end date be after start date
      const endDate = new Date(post_event_info.end_date.year, post_event_info.end_date.month - 1, post_event_info.end_date.day);
      if (endDate < startDate) {
        //modal error
        document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
        document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "A data de término do evento deve ser igual ou posterior à data de início.";
        $('#post-return').modal('show');
        console.log("error C");
        return false;
      }

    }


    //title
    if (!post_event_info.title){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira um título para o evento.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error B");
      return false;
    }


    // title must be at most 58 characters
    if (post_event_info.title.length > 58){
      //modal error
      document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
      document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "O título do evento deve ter no máximo 58 caracteres.";
      $('#post-return').modal('show');
      console.log("error C");
      return false;
    }




    return true;
    
  }


  function send_publish_post(){
    console.log("continue pos2");


const description = document.getElementById('postDescription').value;
const media = JSON.stringify(window.selected_images);
const publish_now = state.post_now;
const schedule_date = $('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').startDate.format('YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm');
const local_timezone = moment.tz.guess();
const local_offset = moment.tz(local_timezone).format('Z');
const metadata = getExifData();

const location_id = document.getElementById("business-id-handler").innerHTML;


console.log("continue pos2");

let call_to_action = {};
if (selected_button_value !== 'none') {

    if (!document.getElementById('buttonUrl').value && selected_button_value !== 'CALL') {
      // if call to action is not call and there is no url
        //modal error
        document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
        document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira uma URL para o botão de chamada para ação.";
        $('#post-return').modal('show');
        console.log("error A");
        return;
    }

    call_to_action = {
        actionType: selected_button_value,
        url: selected_button_value == 'CALL' ? "" : document.getElementById('buttonUrl').value
    };
}


document.getElementById("publish_now").disabled = true;


$.ajax({
    data: {
      create_post: true,
      description: description,
      media: media,
      publish_now: publish_now,
      schedule_date: schedule_date,
      local_timezone: local_timezone,
      local_offset: local_offset,
      editing_post: editing_post,
      topic_type: post_type,
      call_to_action: JSON.stringify(call_to_action),
      post_offer_info: JSON.stringify(post_offer_info),
      post_event_info: JSON.stringify(post_event_info),
      metadata: JSON.stringify(metadata),
      location_id: location_id,

    },
    type: "POST",
    url: window.location.href
})
.done(function(data) {

  requestEvolution(location_id);
  
  
  
  console.log(data);
  if (data.success){



    //change_posts_view_type(global_view_type);

    reset_modal_and_new_post_data();
    //close modal 
    $('#postModal').modal('hide');
    document.getElementById("publish_now").disabled = false;

    document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = data.title;
    document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = data.message;
    $('#post-return').modal('show');
      //modal on close refresh

    document.getElementById("close-modal-success").addEventListener("click", function(){
      //location.reload();
      
    });


  }else{
    document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = data.title;
    document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = data.error;
    $('#post-return').modal('show');
    document.getElementById("publish_now").disabled = false;
  }

  




});

  }


      function publish_post(){

        console.log("publishing post");

        // Final validation before publish
        if (!validateBeforePublish()) {
            console.log("validation failed before publish");
            return;
        }

        if (post_type === "offer"){
          fill_post_offer_info();
          if (!verify_needed_fields_offer()){
            console.log("error offer info");
            return;
          }
        }else if (post_type === "event"){
          fill_post_event_info();
          if (!verify_needed_fields_event()){
            console.log("error event info");
            return;
          }
        }


        // if CTA is not none, check if url is valid
        if (selected_button_value !== 'none') {
          if (!isValidUrl(document.getElementById('buttonUrl').value) && selected_button_value !== 'CALL') {
            //modal error
            document.getElementById('post-return-label').innerText = "Erro";
            document.getElementById('post-return-modal-body').innerHTML = "Por favor, insira uma URL válida para o botão de chamada para ação.";
            $('#post-return').modal('show');
            console.log("error A");
            return;
          }
        }



        console.log("continue pos");



        //verify post_type and call the verification function


        const maxHeight = 100; // Altura máxima para a thumbnail

        if (window.selected_images.length === 0) {
            // Se não houver imagens selecionadas, exibe um erro
            console.error('Nenhuma imagem selecionada');
            send_publish_post();
            return;
        }


      // Faz um loop sobre os objetos em selected_images
      window.selected_images.forEach((image, index) => {
      createThumbnail(image.url, maxHeight)
      .then(thumbnail => {
        image.thumbnail = thumbnail; // Adiciona a thumbnail ao objeto
            if (index === window.selected_images.length - 1) {
                // Se for o último item, exibe a lista
                console.log(window.selected_images); // Exibe a lista com as thumbnails adicionadas
        }

        //send post to server
        send_publish_post();



            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Erro ao criar thumbnail:', error);
            });
    });




      
  
      }
  
      document.getElementById("publish_now").addEventListener("click", function(){
        try {
    publish_post();
} catch (e) {
    alert("Ocorreu um erro: " + e.message); // Exibe o erro no alert
    throw e; // Relança o erro para que possa ser tratado em outro lugar
}

      })

      function extractErrorReason(errorMessage) {
    try {
        // Extrai a parte relevante da mensagem de erro
        const match = errorMessage.match(/Details: \"(\[.*\])\"/);
        if (match && match[1]) {
            const errorDetails = JSON.parse(match[1].replace(/'/g, '"'));
            if (errorDetails[0] && errorDetails[0].errorDetails) {
                return errorDetails[0].errorDetails.map((err, index) => `${index + 1}. ${err.message}`).join('<br>');
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {
        return 'Erro ao extrair detalhes';
    }
    return 'Nenhum detalhe encontrado';
}

      function get_error_message(post_data){

        const error_message = post_data.creation_response;
        let error_pretty = "";

        if (error_message.includes("Creating Offer and Product posts is not enabled for this location")){
            error_pretty = "A criação de atualizações do tipo ofertas não está habilitada para este local. Entre em contato com o suporte para mais informações.";
        }

        if (error_message.includes("Image format is not supported.")){
          error_pretty = "Formato de imagem não suportado. Por favor, selecione uma imagem no formato PNG ou JPEG/JPG.";
        }

        if (error_message.includes("The link you’ve entered is invalid")){
          error_pretty = "O link inserido é inválido. Por favor, insira um link válido.";
        }

        if (error_message.includes("Image too small. Got")){
          error_pretty = "A imagem é muito pequena. Por favor, selecione uma imagem com pelo menos 250 pixels de largura e 250 pixels de altura.";
        }

        if (error_message.includes("mage bytes too small. Got")){
          error_pretty = "A imagem é muito pequena. Por favor, selecione uma imagem com pelo menos 10 KB.";
        }



        error_reason = extractErrorReason(error_message);


        return {
          error_pretty: error_pretty,
          error_reason: error_reason
        }

      }

      function send_error_to_support(post_id, error_message){
        error_message = error_message.replaceAll("'", "").replaceAll('"', '');
        const message = `Olá, tudo bem? 

Preciso de ajuda com a postagem de ID ${post_id}.

Ocorreu um erro ao tentar publicar a postagem.

Mensagem de erro: ${error_message}`;

//close modal
$('#postModal').modal('hide');


        $crisp.push(["do", "chat:open", []])


 // Depois, aguardar um pouco e enviar a mensagem
 setTimeout(() => {
  $crisp.push(["do", "message:send", ["text", message]]);
    }, 500); // Pequeno delay para garantir que o chat já foi aberto



      }

      function open_post_success_modal(post_data, error){

        if (error){
          document.getElementById("post-feedback-view-on-google-holder").style.display = "none";
          document.getElementById("post-feedback-logo").style.display = "none";

          const error_message_dict = get_error_message(post_data);

          const error_message = error_message_dict.error_pretty ? error_message_dict.error_pretty : error_message_dict.error_reason;

          const support_btn = error_message_dict.error_pretty ? "" : `<button class="btn" style="background-color: #0099ee; color:white;" onclick="send_error_to_support('${post_data["id"]}', '${error_message}')">Enviar erro ao suporte</button>`;

          document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
          
          ${error_message}

          <br><br>

          <div style="display: flex; justify-content: center;">

            ${support_btn}

            </div>



          
          `;

        }else{
          document.getElementById("post-feedback-view-on-google-holder").style.display = "block";
          document.getElementById("post-feedback-logo").style.display = "block";
          document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerText = "Parabéns, sua postagem foi enviada com sucesso";
        }

        console.log("POST DATA success",post_data);
        const metadata_forced_use_by_user = post_data.metadata_forced_use_by_user;

        if (metadata_forced_use_by_user){
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "block";

          const metadata = JSON.parse(post_data.image_metadata);

          console.log("metadata",metadata);


          let metadata_tooltip = "Metadados da imagem:<br>";

          if (metadata.title){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Título:</b> " + metadata.title + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.description){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Descrição:</b> " + metadata.description + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.keywords){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Palavras-chave:</b> " + metadata.keywords + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.gpsLatitude && metadata.gpsLongitude){
            const gpsLink = "https://www.google.com/maps/search/" + metadata.gpsLatitude + "," + metadata.gpsLongitude;
            metadata_tooltip += "<a target='_blank' href='"+gpsLink+"'><b>GPS:</b> " + metadata.gpsLatitude + ", " + metadata.gpsLongitude + "</a><br>";
          }

          if (metadata.fileName){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Nome do arquivo:</b> " + metadata.fileName + "<br>";
          }

          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-original-title", metadata_tooltip);
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-toggle", "tooltip");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-placement", "right");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("title", "");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-html", "true");

          const iconElement = document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata");


          // prevent tooltip to close on hover without trigger manual
          // Inicializa o tooltip com eventos personalizados
          $(iconElement).tooltip({ trigger: 'manual' });

          iconElement.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
            $(this).tooltip('show'); // Mostra o tooltip quando o mouse entra
          });

          iconElement.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
            // Aguarda um curto intervalo para verificar se o mouse está sobre o tooltip
            setTimeout(() => {
              if (!$('.tooltip:hover').length) {
                $(this).tooltip('hide'); // Fecha o tooltip se o mouse não estiver sobre ele
              }
            }, 100);
          });

          


        }else{
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "none";
        }


        document.getElementById('card-success').style.display = "flex";
        document.getElementById('card-scheduled').style.display = "none";

        

        document.getElementById('view-on-google-calendar-edit').onclick = function(){
          window.open(post_data.postSearchUrl, '_blank');
        }

        post_data.media = JSON.parse(post_data.media);


        //set description
        document.getElementById('postDescription').value = post_data.summary;
        //fire event to update char count
        document.getElementById('postDescription').dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));


if (!post_data.schedule_date){
  post_data.schedule_date = post_data.moment_of_submission;
}

try{

call_to_action = JSON.parse(post_data.call_to_action);
document.querySelector(`[data-value="${call_to_action.actionType}"]`).click();

document.getElementById("buttonUrl").value = call_to_action.url;

}catch{}

// Garante que a data seja interpretada exatamente como está, sem alterações de fuso horário
const localDate = moment.parseZone(post_data.schedule_date);

// Formatar a data no estilo DD/MM/YYYY HH:MM
const formattedDate = localDate.format("DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm");

// Exibir a data formatada no elemento HTML
document.getElementById('datetime-post-success').innerText = formattedDate;





// Atualiza os valores no input
//timezone?
$('input[name="birthday"]').val(localDate.format('DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm'));
$('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setStartDate(localDate);
$('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setEndDate(localDate);

        //set images - Load from server instead of base64 from DB
        // For published posts, thumbnail is displayed via recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url
        // No need to populate selected_images as updateImagePreview is not called for SUCCESS posts

        // set thumbnail
        //open modal
        editing_post = post_data.id;


        $('#postModal').modal('show');

        recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url(post_data.thumbnail);



      }

      function open_post_retry_modal(post_data){
        // Modal para posts com status RETRY - mostra informação de que está tentando novamente
        document.getElementById("post-feedback-view-on-google-holder").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("post-feedback-logo").style.display = "none";
        
        document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
          <div style="text-align: center;">
            <i class="fa-solid fa-clock" style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #FF6600;"></i>
            <p style="color: #333; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 12px; line-height: 1.4;">
              Sua postagem está sendo publicada automaticamente
            </p>
            <p style="color: #666; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0; line-height: 1.4;">
              Isso pode levar alguns minutos. Você pode fechar este modal <span id="secret-retry-trigger">e</span> voltar mais tarde para verificar.
            </p>
          </div>
        `;

        console.log("POST DATA retry", post_data);
        const metadata_forced_use_by_user = post_data.metadata_forced_use_by_user;

        if (metadata_forced_use_by_user){
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "block";

          const metadata = JSON.parse(post_data.image_metadata);
          console.log("metadata",metadata);

          let metadata_tooltip = "Metadados da imagem:<br>";

          if (metadata.title){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Título:</b> " + metadata.title + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.description){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Descrição:</b> " + metadata.description + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.keywords){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Palavras-chave:</b> " + metadata.keywords + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.gpsLatitude && metadata.gpsLongitude){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Localização:</b> " + metadata.gpsLatitude + ", " + metadata.gpsLongitude + "<br>";
          }

          $("#icon-location-metadata").attr("data-original-title", metadata_tooltip);
        }else{
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "none";
        }

        // Mostrar card de sucesso/feedback com informações do retry
        document.getElementById('card-success').style.display = "flex";
        document.getElementById('card-scheduled').style.display = "none";

        // Preencher informações do post
        document.getElementById("postDescription").value = post_data.summary;
        
        // Preencher o preview do post
        const previewText = document.getElementById("previewText");
        if (previewText) {
            previewText.innerText = post_data.summary;
        }
        
        // Esconder o ícone megafone se há texto
        const previewIcon = document.getElementById("previewIconMegaphone");
        if (previewIcon && post_data.summary) {
            previewIcon.style.display = "none";
        }

        // Load images from server instead of base64 from DB
        // For retry posts, thumbnail is displayed via recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url
        // No need to populate selected_images as updateImagePreview is not called for RETRY posts

        // set thumbnail
        //open modal
        editing_post = post_data.id;

        $('#postModal').modal('show');

        if (post_data.thumbnail) {
            recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url(post_data.thumbnail);
        }

        // Secret double-click on "e" for manual retry
        let secretRetryClickCount = 0;
        let secretRetryTimer;
        
        document.getElementById('secret-retry-trigger').addEventListener('click', function() {
            secretRetryClickCount++;
            
            if (secretRetryClickCount === 1) {
                secretRetryTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                    secretRetryClickCount = 0;
                }, 1000); // 1 segundo para 2 cliques
            }
            
            if (secretRetryClickCount === 2) {
                clearTimeout(secretRetryTimer);
                secretRetryClickCount = 0;
                
                // Executar retry manual
                performManualRetry(post_data.id);
            }
        });
      }

      function open_post_edition_modal(post_data){
        console.log("POST DATA",post_data);

        document.getElementById('card-success').style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById('card-scheduled').style.display = "flex";
        
        post_data.media = JSON.parse(post_data.media);





        if (post_data.topicType=="OFFER"){
            document.getElementById("offer-item-nav").click();
            post_data_offer_info = JSON.parse(post_data.post_offer_info);

            document.getElementById("postTitleOptional").value = post_data_offer_info.title;
            document.getElementById("offerCoupomCode").value = post_data_offer_info.coupom_code;
            document.getElementById("offerCoupomRedeemUrl").value = post_data_offer_info.coupom_redeem_url;
            document.getElementById("offerTermsAndConditions").value = post_data_offer_info.terms_and_conditions;

            // Formatar números para terem dois dígitos
            function padZero(value) {
                return value.toString().padStart(2, '0');
            }

            // Data de início
            const start_date = post_data_offer_info.start_date;
            const start_date_str = start_date.year + "-" + padZero(start_date.month) + "-" + padZero(start_date.day);
            console.error("start_date", start_date_str);
            $('#offerStartDate').val(start_date_str);

            // Data de fim
            const end_date = post_data_offer_info.end_date;
            const end_date_str = end_date.year + "-" + padZero(end_date.month) + "-" + padZero(end_date.day);
            console.error("end_date", end_date_str);
            $('#offerEndDate').val(end_date_str);

            
        }else if (post_data.topicType=="EVENT"){
            document.getElementById("event-item-nav").click();
            post_data_event_info = JSON.parse(post_data.post_event_info);

            document.getElementById("postTitleOptional").value = post_data_event_info.title;

            //date start to input #eventStartDate
            const start_date = post_data_event_info.start_date;
            const start_date_str = start_date.year + "-" + start_date.month + "-" + start_date.day;
            $('#eventStartDate').val(start_date_str);

            //date end to input #eventEndDate
            const end_date = post_data_event_info.end_date;
            const end_date_str = end_date.year + "-" + end_date.month + "-" + end_date.day;
            $('#eventEndDate').val(end_date_str);

            //hour start to input #eventStartHour
            const start_hour = post_data_event_info.start_hour;


            let start_hour_str = `00:00`;
            if (start_hour){
            // Adiciona zeros à esquerda para garantir o formato correto
            const hours = String(start_hour.hours).padStart(2, '0');
            const minutes = String(start_hour.minutes).padStart(2, '0');
            start_hour_str = `${hours}:${minutes}`;
            }

            

            



            // Define o valor no campo de entrada
            $('#eventStartHour').val(start_hour_str);


            //hour end to input #eventEndHour
            const end_hour = post_data_event_info.end_hour;
            let end_hour_str = `00:00`;
            if (end_hour){
                     
                // Adiciona zeros à esquerda para garantir o formato correto  
              const hours_end = String(end_hour.hours).padStart(2, '0');
              const minutes_end = String(end_hour.minutes).padStart(2, '0');

              // Formata a string no formato esperado pelo campo de entrada
              end_hour_str = `${hours_end}:${minutes_end}`;
            }
              
           

            // Define o valor no campo de entrada
            $('#eventEndHour').val(end_hour_str);
        }










        const metadata_forced_use_by_user = post_data.metadata_forced_use_by_user;

        if (metadata_forced_use_by_user){
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "block";

          const metadata = JSON.parse(post_data.image_metadata);

          console.log("metadata",metadata);

          //add metadata to modal matadate section
          document.getElementById('title').value = metadata.title;
          document.getElementById('description').value = metadata.description;
          document.getElementById('keywords').value = metadata.keywords;
          document.getElementById('gpsLatitude').value = metadata.gpsLatitude;
          document.getElementById('gpsLongitude').value = metadata.gpsLongitude;

          file_title_global = metadata.fileName;
          document.getElementById('fileName').value = metadata.fileName;




          // select metadata checkbox
          document.getElementById('addMetadata').checked = true;
          //fire toggle event 
          document.getElementById('addMetadata').dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));


          let metadata_tooltip = "Metadados da imagem:<br>";

          if (metadata.title){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Título:</b> " + metadata.title + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.description){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Descrição:</b> " + metadata.description + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.keywords){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Palavras-chave:</b> " + metadata.keywords + "<br>";
          }

          if (metadata.gpsLatitude && metadata.gpsLongitude){
            const gpsLink = "https://www.google.com/maps/search/" + metadata.gpsLatitude + "," + metadata.gpsLongitude;
            metadata_tooltip += "<a target='_blank' href='"+gpsLink+"'><b>GPS:</b> " + metadata.gpsLatitude + ", " + metadata.gpsLongitude + "</a><br>";
          }

          if (metadata.fileName){
            metadata_tooltip += "<b>Nome do arquivo:</b> " + metadata.fileName + "<br>";
          }

          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-original-title", metadata_tooltip);
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-toggle", "tooltip");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-placement", "right");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("title", "");
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").setAttribute("data-html", "true");

          const iconElement = document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata");


          // prevent tooltip to close on hover without trigger manual
          // Inicializa o tooltip com eventos personalizados
          $(iconElement).tooltip({ trigger: 'manual' });

          iconElement.addEventListener('mouseenter', function () {
            $(this).tooltip('show'); // Mostra o tooltip quando o mouse entra
          });

          iconElement.addEventListener('mouseleave', function () {
            // Aguarda um curto intervalo para verificar se o mouse está sobre o tooltip
            setTimeout(() => {
              if (!$('.tooltip:hover').length) {
                $(this).tooltip('hide'); // Fecha o tooltip se o mouse não estiver sobre ele
              }
            }, 100);
          });

          


        }else{
          document.getElementById("icon-location-metadata").style.display = "none";
          document.getElementById('addMetadata').checked = false;
          document.getElementById('title').value = "";
          document.getElementById('description').value = "";
          document.getElementById('keywords').value = "";
        }







        try{
            call_to_action = JSON.parse(post_data.call_to_action);
            if (!call_to_action.actionType){
              call_to_action.actionType = "none";
              document.getElementById("buttonUrl").value = "";
            }else{

              document.getElementById("buttonUrl").value = call_to_action.url;
            }
            
            document.querySelector(`[data-value="${call_to_action.actionType}"]`).click();
        }catch {}

            

        //set description
        document.getElementById('postDescription').value = post_data.summary;
        //fire event to update char count
        document.getElementById('postDescription').dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));


        //set date
// Define a data corretamente no input sem conversão de fuso horário
// Garante que a data seja interpretada exatamente como está, sem alterações de fuso horário
const localDate = moment.parseZone(post_data.schedule_date);

// Atualiza os valores no input
//timezone?
$('input[name="birthday"]').val(localDate.format('DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm'));
$('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setStartDate(localDate);
$('input[name="birthday"]').data('daterangepicker').setEndDate(localDate);

        //set images - Load from server instead of base64 from DB
        // For scheduled/pending posts being edited, load full image from server
        if (post_data.thumbnail) {
            const imageUrl = `https://app.gbpcheck.com/manager/posts/media-server/${post_data.unique_media_uuid}.jpg`;
            selected_images = [{
                url: imageUrl,
                name: post_data.unique_media_uuid || post_data.id,
                thumbnail: `https://app.gbpcheck.com/manager/posts/media-server-thumbanail/${post_data.thumbnail}`
            }];
        } else {
            selected_images = [];
        }

        //open modal
        editing_post = post_data.id;



        if (post_data.publish_now){
          $('input[name="birthday"]').val(translations["Agora"]);
          state.post_now = true;
        }else{
            state.post_now = false;
            }





        $('#postModal').modal('show');

        // Manually trigger carousel update to show the loaded image
        manuallyUpdateCarousel();

        


      }

      function get_post_for_edition(post_id){
        $.ajax({
            data: {
                get_post_by_id: true,
                post_id: post_id
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            console.log("post for editing", data);


            if (data.post.status == "SCHEDULED"){
              open_post_edition_modal(data.post);
              // Only call updateImagePreview for SCHEDULED posts (they use manuallyUpdateCarousel)
              updateImagePreview();
            }else if (data.post.status == "SUCCESS"){
              open_post_success_modal(data.post, false);
              // SUCCESS posts use recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url, don't call updateImagePreview
            }else if (data.post.status == "ERROR"){
              open_post_success_modal(data.post, true);
              // ERROR posts use recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url, don't call updateImagePreview
            }else if (data.post.status == "RETRY"){
              open_post_retry_modal(data.post);
              // RETRY posts use recreate_images_selected_carousel_with_url, don't call updateImagePreview
            }



        });


      }


      function update_event_date(event_id, new_date){

        $.ajax({
            data: {
                update_event_date: true,
                event_id: event_id,
                new_date: new_date
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            if (data.success){
              //get_posts_for_dates_interval();
              set_calendar_dimensions();
            }
        });
      }



      function publish_existing_post_now(post_id){
        $.ajax({
            data: {
                post_now_scheduled: true,
                post_id: post_id
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            console.log("post_now", data);
            get_posts_for_list_view();
        });
      }

      function performManualRetry(post_id) {
        
        // Update modal message to show retry in progress
        document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
          <div style="text-align: center;">
            <i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin" style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #FF6600;"></i>
            <p style="color: #333; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 12px; line-height: 1.4;">
              Tentando publicar novamente...
            </p>
            <p style="color: #666; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0; line-height: 1.4;">
              Aguarde, processando sua publicação.
            </p>
          </div>
        `;
        
        $.ajax({
            data: {
                post_now_scheduled: true,
                post_id: post_id
            },
            type: "POST",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            
            // Process response and update UI
            if (data.success) {
                // Success - update modal
                document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
                  <div style="text-align: center;">
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-check-circle" style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #28a745;"></i>
                    <p style="color: #333; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 12px; line-height: 1.4;">
                      Publicação realizada com sucesso!
                    </p>
                    <p style="color: #666; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0; line-height: 1.4;">
                      Sua postagem foi publicada no Google My Business.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                `;
                
                // Show success options
                if (data.post_id_created && data.postSearchUrl) {
                    document.getElementById("post-feedback-view-on-google-holder").style.display = "block";
                    document.getElementById("view-on-google").href = data.postSearchUrl;
                }
                
            } else {
                // Error - show error message
                document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
                  <div style="text-align: center;">
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-exclamation-triangle" style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #dc3545;"></i>
                    <p style="color: #333; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 12px; line-height: 1.4;">
                      Falha na publicação
                    </p>
                    <p style="color: #666; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0; line-height: 1.4;">
                      ${data.message || 'Erro desconhecido na publicação.'}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                `;
            }
            
            // Refresh list after 2 seconds
            setTimeout(() => {
                get_posts_for_list_view();
            }, 2000);
            
        }).fail(function(xhr, status, error) {
            console.error("🔄 Manual retry failed:", error);
            
            // Show error message
            document.getElementById("post-feedback-message").innerHTML = `
              <div style="text-align: center;">
                <i class="fa-solid fa-exclamation-triangle" style="font-size: 36px; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #dc3545;"></i>
                <p style="color: #333; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 500; margin-bottom: 12px; line-height: 1.4;">
                  Erro na tentativa de publicação
                </p>
                <p style="color: #666; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0; line-height: 1.4;">
                  Ocorreu um erro ao tentar publicar. Tente novamente mais tarde.
                </p>
              </div>
            `;
        });
      }

      function delete_post_by_id(post_id){
        $.ajax({
            data: {
                delete_post: true,
                post_id: post_id
            },
            type: "DELETE",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            console.log("delete_post", data);
            get_posts_for_list_view();
        });
      }


      function delete_post(){
        if (!editing_post){
            return;
        }


        $.ajax({
            data: {
                delete_post: true,
                post_id: editing_post
            },
            type: "DELETE",
            url: window.location.href
        }).done(function(data) {
            console.log("delete_post", data);

            if (data.success){
              get_posts_for_dates_interval();
              reset_modal_and_new_post_data();
              $('#postModal').modal('hide');
            }
        });
      }

      document.getElementById("cancel_schedule").addEventListener("click", function(){
        delete_post();
      });

      document.getElementById("cancel_now").addEventListener("click", function(){
        reset_modal_and_new_post_data();
        $('#postModal').modal('hide');
      });

      $('#postModal').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
        if (editing_post){
          document.getElementById("cancel_schedule").style.display = "block";
        }else{
          document.getElementById("cancel_schedule").style.display = "none";
        }



      });



      



      // Detecta o fechamento de qualquer modal
$('.modal').on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
    if ($('.modal:visible').length) {  // Verifica se há algum modal ainda visível
        $('body').addClass('modal-open'); // Se houver, re-adiciona a classe modal-open
    }
});
