function getRandomCoordinate(lat, lng, minDistance, maxDistance) {
    lat = parseFloat(lat);
    lng = parseFloat(lng);
    // Converter metros para graus (1 grau de latitude ≈ 111320 metros)
    const metersToDegrees = 1 / 111320;

    // Gerar deslocamento aleatório em metros
    const randomDistance = Math.random() * (maxDistance - minDistance) + minDistance;

    // Converter a distância para graus
    const randomOffsetLat = randomDistance * metersToDegrees;

    // Ajustar para longitude, levando em conta a latitude atual
    const randomOffsetLng = randomDistance * metersToDegrees / Math.cos(lat * (Math.PI / 180));

    // Aleatoriamente escolher direção positiva ou negativa
    let newLat = lat + (Math.random() < 0.5 ? -randomOffsetLat : randomOffsetLat);
    let newLng = lng + (Math.random() < 0.5 ? -randomOffsetLng : randomOffsetLng);

    // only 7 decimal places
    newLat = newLat.toFixed(7);
    newLng = newLng.toFixed(7);

    return { lat: newLat, lng: newLng };
}



function go_to_maps_reference(){
  const lat = document.getElementById('gpsLatitude').value;
  const lng = document.getElementById('gpsLongitude').value;
  const url = "https://www.google.com/maps/search/" + lat + "," + lng;
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.target = "_blank";
  a.click();
}

// Image upload event listeners
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const uploadInput = document.getElementById('upload-media-input');
    const dropArea = document.getElementById('drop-area');
    
    // Monitor text changes to update button states
    const postDescription = document.getElementById('postDescription');
    if (postDescription) {
        postDescription.addEventListener('input', updatePublishButtonStates);
        postDescription.addEventListener('change', updatePublishButtonStates);
        postDescription.addEventListener('keyup', updatePublishButtonStates);
    }
    
    // Initial button state check
    updatePublishButtonStates();

    // File input change event
    uploadInput.addEventListener('change', async function(e) {
        const files = Array.from(e.target.files);
        
        for (const file of files) {
            await validateAndAddImage(file);
        }
        
        // Clear input so same file can be selected again
        e.target.value = '';
    });

    // Drag and drop events
    dropArea.addEventListener('dragover', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        dropArea.classList.add('drag-over');
        dropArea.style.borderColor = '#0099ee';
        dropArea.style.backgroundColor = '#f0f8ff';
    });

    dropArea.addEventListener('dragleave', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        
        // Only remove styles if leaving the drop area entirely
        if (!dropArea.contains(e.relatedTarget)) {
            dropArea.classList.remove('drag-over');
            dropArea.style.borderColor = '#ccc';
            dropArea.style.backgroundColor = '';
        }
    });

    dropArea.addEventListener('drop', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        
        console.log('🎯 DROP EVENT - Starting drag and drop upload');
        console.log('🎯 Images before drop:', window.selected_images.length);
        
        dropArea.classList.remove('drag-over');
        dropArea.style.borderColor = '#ccc';
        dropArea.style.backgroundColor = '';
        
        const files = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files);
        
        // Filter only image files
        const imageFiles = files.filter(file => file.type.startsWith('image/'));
        
        if (imageFiles.length !== files.length) {
            showValidationError('Alguns arquivos não são imagens e foram ignorados.', true);
        }
        
        for (const file of imageFiles) {
            console.log('🎯 Processing dropped file:', file.name);
            await validateAndAddImage(file);
        }
        
        console.log('🎯 Images after drop:', window.selected_images.length);
    });

    // Prevent default drag behaviors on window
    ['dragenter', 'dragover', 'dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
        window.addEventListener(eventName, function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
        }, false);
    });

    // Add CSS for drag-over state
    const style = document.createElement('style');
    style.textContent = `
        .drag-over {
            border-color: #0099ee !important;
            background-color: #f0f8ff !important;
            transform: scale(1.02);
            transition: all 0.2s ease;
        }
        
        .validation-error {
            animation: shake 0.5s ease-in-out;
        }
        
        @keyframes shake {
            0%, 20%, 40%, 60%, 80% { transform: translateX(0); }
            10%, 30%, 50%, 70% { transform: translateX(-5px); }
            15%, 35%, 55%, 75% { transform: translateX(5px); }
        }
        
        .image-validation-badge {
            position: absolute;
            top: 5px;
            right: 5px;
            background: #28a745;
            color: white;
            border-radius: 50%;
            width: 20px;
            height: 20px;
            font-size: 12px;
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            z-index: 10;
        }
        
        .image-validation-badge.error {
            background: #dc3545;
        }
    `;
    document.head.appendChild(style);
});

// Secret debug feature - 4 clicks in 2 seconds on share icon
let secretClickCount = 0;
let secretClickTimer = null;

function handleSecretDebugClick() {
  secretClickCount++;
  
  if (secretClickCount === 1) {
    // Start 2-second timer
    secretClickTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      secretClickCount = 0; // Reset if 2 seconds pass
    }, 2000);
  }
  
  if (secretClickCount === 4) {
    // Clear timer and reset counter
    clearTimeout(secretClickTimer);
    secretClickCount = 0;
    
    // Get current editing post ID
    if (editing_post) {
      // Navigate to debug page
      window.location.href = '/manager/posts-debug/' + editing_post;
    } else {
      console.log('No post selected for debug');
    }
  }
}

<script>
   document.getElementById("welcome-msg-heart").onclick = ()=>{
        //Change message throw list options
        welcome_msgs= [translations["BEM VINDO"], translations["BEM VINDA"]];
        let welcomeMsg = document.getElementById("welcome-msg-txt");
        let welcomeMsgText = welcomeMsg.innerText;
        let index = welcome_msgs.indexOf(welcomeMsgText);
        if(index == welcome_msgs.length-1){
            index = 0;
        }else{
            index++;
        }
        welcomeMsg.innerText = welcome_msgs[index];

    }

    let timer_pdf_download;



function remove_download_pdf_user_message(){
    clearInterval(timer_pdf_download);
    if (document.getElementById("generating-pdf-custom-message")){
        document.getElementById("generating-pdf-custom-message").remove();
    }
    document.getElementById("dropdownMenuButtonActionsID").classList.remove("disabled");
}

    function set_download_pdf_user_message(timer){
        if (document.getElementById("generating-pdf-custom-message")){
            return;
        }
        




        document.getElementById("dropdownMenuButtonActionsID").classList.add("disabled");


        if (!timer){
            timer = 10;
        }


        const custom_html = `
        <div id="generating-pdf-custom-message" style="display: contents;">
            
            &nbsp;&nbsp;

            <div style="display:inline-flex; justify-content:center; align-items:center;">

                <span id="generating-pdf-custom-message-timer-msg" style="margin-top:-2px; margin-left:1px; width:100%; text-align:right; font-size:13px;">Preparando o Download...<span id="generating-pdf-custom-message-timer">&nbsp;${timer}</span> </span>
                &nbsp;&nbsp;
                <i class="icon-spinner3 spinner" style="font-size:15px;"></i>

            </div>
            
            </div>

            `;


        // add html
        document.querySelector(".actions-bar div").insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', custom_html);

        timer_pdf_download = setInterval(()=>{
            timer--;
            document.getElementById("generating-pdf-custom-message-timer").innerText = timer;
            if (timer == 0){
                document.getElementById("generating-pdf-custom-message-timer-msg").innerText = "Pode demorar mais um pouco...";
                clearInterval(timer_pdf_download);
            }
        }, 1000);
    }




    function open_modal_support_based_on_code(){


    }


var global_modal_support = [];

function open_chat_sup(){
    let el=document.querySelector('[data-pane-animate-entrance]'); if(el){el.click(); return;};
    el=document.querySelector('#crisp-chatbox > div > a'); if(el){el.click(); return;};


}
function get_support(){
    $.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: "/help",
        data:{
            "route": window.location.pathname
        }
    }).done(function(data) {
        //console.log("rota",data)
        
        if (data){

            console.log(data);

            let complete_html = `
            <div class="dropdown" id="help-dropdown-ms">
                <button style="background:#7D7D7D; padding: 5px 10px 5px 10px; color:white;" class="btn dropdown-toggle" type="button" id="dropdownMenuButtonActionsIDHelp" data-toggle="dropdown" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">
                    Ajuda
                </button>
                <div class="actions-dropdown dropdown-menu" aria-labelledby="dropdownMenuButtonActionsIDHelp" id="support-dropdown-body-help">
                    ${data.html_structure}

                    <div class="dropdown-divider"></div>
                    <a class="dropdown-item" href="#" onclick="open_chat_sup();"><i class="icon-bubbles3"></i>Falar com Suporte via Chat</a>

                </div>
            </div>


            
            `;
            document.querySelector(".actions-bar > div").insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', complete_html);

            global_modal_support = JSON.parse(data.modal_structure);

            document.querySelectorAll("[data-help-modal-code]").forEach((el)=>{
                el.onclick = ()=>{
                    let code = el.getAttribute("data-help-modal-code");

                    console.log(code)
                    let modal = null;

                    global_modal_support.forEach((m)=>{
                        if (m.code == code){
                            modal = m;
                        }
                    });

                    console.log(modal)
                    if (modal){
                        let modal_html = modal.html;
                        let modal_title = modal.title;
                        let modal_size = modal.size;



                        let global_modal_test = document.getElementById('modal-support-test');

                        global_modal_test.querySelector('.modal-title').innerText = modal_title;
                        global_modal_test.querySelector('.modal-body').innerHTML = modal_html;

                        //set size
                        let modal_dialog = global_modal_test.querySelector('.modal-dialog');
                        modal_dialog.classList.remove('modal-sm');
                        modal_dialog.classList.remove('modal-lg');
                        modal_dialog.classList.remove('modal-xl');

                        if (modal_size == 'small'){
                            modal_dialog.classList.add('modal-sm');
                        }else if (modal_size == 'medium'){
                            modal_dialog.classList.add('modal-lg');
                        }else if (modal_size == 'large'){
                            modal_dialog.classList.add('modal-xl');
                        }

                        $('#modal-support-test').modal('show');

                }


                }
            });


        }


    });
}


get_support();
</script>
